Question #1 (ID: 209593)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Michael Madhusudandatt was (a) — popular 19 th century Bengali poet and dramatist. He was born in (b) — Sagardari on (c) — bank of (d) — Kopotaksho river, (e) — village in Keshobpur Upazilla under Jessore district. From (f) — early age, Dutt aspired to be (g) — Englishman in form and manner. Though he was born in (h) — sophisticated Hindu family, he took Christianity arousing (i) — anger of his family. He contributed much to (j) — development of Bangali literature.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) a (b) x  (c) the (d) the (e) a (f) the/ x (g) an (h) a (i) the / x (j) the

Explanation:
এই বাক্যে (a) অংশে 'a' ব্যবহার করা যুক্তিযুক্ত কারণ এখানে তিনি একজন সাধারণ/নির্দিষ্ট নয় এমন উনিশ শতকের বাংলা কবি ও নাট্যকার হিসেবে আলোচিত; (b) অংশে 'in' লাগে কারণ জন্মস্থান বলা হচ্ছে (born in Sagardari)। (c) ও (d) অংশে 'the' প্রয়োজন — 'on the bank of the Kopotaksha river' — কারণ এখানে নির্দিষ্ট তীর ও নির্দিষ্ট নদীর কথা বলা হচ্ছে; (e) অংশে 'a village' ব্যবহার করা হয় কারণ সেটা একটি অজানা/নির্দিষ্ট নয় এমন গ্রাম বোঝায়। (f) ও (g) অংশে 'an' লাগে ('an early age', 'an Englishman') কারণ 'early' ও 'Englishman' স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু; (h) অংশে 'a' (a sophisticated/সম্ভ্রান্ত Hindu family) সঠিক, এবং (i) 'the anger' ও (j) 'the development' এ 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয় কারণ এখানে পরিবারগত রাগ এবং বাংলা সাহিত্যের উন্নয়ন — উভয়ই নির্দিষ্ট বিষয় নির্দেশ করছে।

Question #2 (ID: 209594)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There is a saying that sincerity is (a) — key to success. (b) — person can prosper in life by doing hard work. The man who does not follow (c) — rules of sincerity can never go (d) — long way in (e) — world. Many (f) — man is not conscious of (g) — importance of (h) — sincerity for which they don’t have (i) — benefit of (j) — success. However, we should be sincere to our work if we want to achieve anything notable.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) the (b) A; (c) the; (d) a; (e) the; (f) a; (g) the; (h) x; (i) the; (j) x;

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক — “the”, কারণ “the key to success” নির্দিষ্ট ও স্বতন্ত্র অর্থ দেয়। খ — “a”, কারণ এখানে সাধারণ এক ব্যক্তি বোঝানো হয়েছে। গ — “the”, কারণ নির্দিষ্ট “rules”-এর কথা বলা হচ্ছে। ঘ — “a”, কারণ ইংরেজিতে “go a long way” বলেই অভিব্যক্তি। ঙ — “the”, কারণ “the world” সাধারণভাবে নির্দিষ্ট বিশ্বকে বোঝায়। চ — “a”, কারণ বিশেষজ্ঞ রীতিতে “many a man” ব্যবহার করে একাধিক ব্যক্তিকে নির্দেশ করে। ছ — “the”, কারণ “the importance” এখানে নির্দিষ্ট গুরুত্ব বোঝায়। জ — (কোনো আর্টিকেল নেই), কারণ “sincerity” একটি অপরিমেয়, বিমূর্ত শব্দ। ঝ — “the”, কারণ নির্দিষ্ট “benefit” নির্দেশ করা হয়েছে। ঞ — (কোনো আর্টিকেল নেই), কারণ এখানে “success” বিমূর্তভাবে ব্যবহৃত হয়েছে।

Question #3 (ID: 209595)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Every student wants to do better in (a) — examination. But it is not (b) — easy work. (c) — student has to do something for this. From (d) — very beginning he must be serious. He should read (e) — texts again and again. He must not memorize (f) — answer without knowing the meaning. He must not make notes from (g) — common source. He should have a good (h) — command over English. By doing all these things (i) — student can hope to make a good (j) — result.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Answers: (a) the, (b) an, (c) the, (d) the, (e) his, (f) the, (g) a, (h) a, (i) a, (j) a. 

Explanation: Use the for something definite or already known (the examination, the very beginning, the answer), use a/an for any one of something (use an before a vowel sound), use possessive his for the student’s own texts, and the fixed collocation is “a good command.”

Question #4 (ID: 209596)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) — morning walk is a good habit for all classes of people. It is (b) — simple exercise and good for health and (c) — mentality. In the morning (d) — air is fresh and free from any kind noise and pollution. This pure (e) — environment makes an effect on (f) — walker’s health and mind, when (g) — man enjoys (h) — beauties and solemnity of (i) — nature in (j) — morning.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Answers: (a) A, (b) a, (c) — (no article), (d) the, (e) — (no article), (f) a, (g) a, (h) the, (i) — (no article), (j) the. 

Explanation: Use [math]a[/math] before a singular, countable noun when speaking generally (e.g., "A morning walk", "a simple exercise", "a man"); use [math]the[/math] for something specific or already identified (e.g., "the air", "the beauties"); use no article with abstract or uncountable nouns or after demonstratives (e.g., "health", "mentality", "this pure environment", "nature"). Also "in the morning" is a fixed expression referring to that part of the day.

Question #5 (ID: 209597)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Literacy as (a) — skill was first institutionalized in Mesopotamia, Syria, Egypt and China soon after (b) — art of writing was invented. Education then was not for (c) — general people but (d) — privilege for (e) — chosen (f) — few who took on strategic roles in (g) — running of (h) — state and in religion. In Greece, education became more widespread in about the 5th century BC. (i) — Greeks, however, sent only their (j) — male children to school.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Explanation: Use "a" for one non‑specific item, "the" for something specific or unique, and no article when a possessive (like "their") already marks the noun. Thus (a) is "a" because "skill" is introduced generally; (b) is "the" because "the art of writing" is a specific invention; (c) is "the" and (d) is "a" ("the general people", "a privilege"); (e) is "the" in "the chosen few"; (g) and (h) are "the" in "the running of the state." Finally, (i) is "The" for "The Greeks", and (j) needs no article because "their" already shows possession ("their male children").

Question #6 (ID: 209598)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
My mother is (a) — ideal housewife. She is (b) — affectionate lady. She manages (c) — family very nicely. She hopes to see me happy at (d) Cost of her own life. She does not enjoy (e) — wink of sleep if I fall sick. She is very kind to (f) — poor. She is also (g) — very religious lady. She advises us to follow (h) — path of truth and honesty. (i) — woman like her is very rare. She bears a good moral (j) — character.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Explanation:
a Use "an" because "ideal" begins with a vowel sound.  
b Use "an" because "affectionate" begins with a vowel sound.  
c Use "her" to show the family she specifically manages (possessive).  
d Use "the" in the fixed phrase "the cost of her own life" (a specific cost).  
e Use "a" because the idiom is "a wink of sleep" (any small amount of sleep).  
f Use "the" with "poor" to mean poor people as a group ("the poor").  
g Use "a" because "very" starts with a consonant sound, so "a very religious lady."  
h Use "the" for a specific route or way: "the path of truth and honesty."  
i Use "A" because we mean "a woman like her" (one such woman).  
j Use "a" before "good moral character" because it's a singular, countable noun phrase.

Question #7 (ID: 209599)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Kamal is (a) — HSC examinee this year. He is not (b) — attentive to his lessons. He weak in (c) — English. Moreover, he is (d) — lazy. So his preparation in English is no (e) — month ago before his examination he managed (f) — short suggestion and learnt (g) — day of examination he started for the examination hall (h) — bit earlier. He entered (i) — examination hall with (j) — trembling heart. 2. Complete the text with suitable prepositions.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Explanation:
(a) "an" — use "an" before the vowel sound of "HSC" (pronounced "aitch‑es‑see"), so "an HSC examinee" is correct.
(b) "very" — "attentive to" needs a degree word; "very attentive to" correctly strengthens the adjective.
(c) (no article) — names of languages normally take no article, so "weak in English" (not "the English").
(d) "quite" — "quite lazy" is a natural degree modifier; it correctly describes the extent of his laziness.
(e) "more" — in the phrase "is no more" (or "no more prepared") "more" completes the negative comparison meaning "not any further/adequate."
(f) "a" — singular countable noun "short suggestion" needs the indefinite article "a."
(g) "on the" — the fixed phrase is "on the day (of the) examination."
(h) "a" — "a bit earlier" is the correct idiom to indicate a small amount of time earlier.
(i) "the" — "the examination hall" refers to a specific place, so use the definite article.
(j) "a" — "a trembling heart" is an indefinite noun phrase describing his state as he entered.

Question #8 (ID: 209600)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2016 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once there lived (a) — poor cobbler. He had (b) — rich neighbor. (c) — neighbour possessed (d) ill-health. So, he was (e) — angry man. He was always (f) — unhappy man Once he used to think (g) — richest men to be (h) — happiest men in (i) — World. But his (j) — idea was wrong.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slvoe add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Use "a" before a singular countable noun introduced for the first time, so (a) "a poor cobbler" and (b) "a rich neighbor." Use "the" for a specific person already mentioned and for superlatives, so (c) "the neighbour" and (g)/(h)/(i) "the richest," "the happiest," "the world." Use "an" before words beginning with a vowel sound, so (e) and (f) are "an angry man" and "an unhappy man," and leave blanks where no article is needed with uncountable nouns or after a possessive, so (d) and (j) are left without an article.

Question #9 (ID: 209601)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Though newspaper is not always (a) — unmixed blessing, it is (b) — most useful thing in our life. We rarely think of (c) — day without reading (d) — newspaper. Reading newspaper is one of (e) — good habits of a man. We shall be like (f) — frog in a dark well if we neglect developing this habit. However, some people prefer (g) — electronic media to reading (h) — newspaper. But (i) — newspaper offers more to its readers than (j) — electronic media.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use a "an" because "unmixed" begins with a vowel sound, and b "the" because "most" is a superlative that needs "the".  
Use c "a" for "a day" (any single day) and d "the" because it refers to the specific newspaper one reads.  
Use e "the" in "one of the good habits", f "a" for a single frog, and g, h, i, j "the" because we are referring to the specific/known media or making a particular comparison.

Question #10 (ID: 209602)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Mosquito menace is one of (a) — most talked topics. (b) — fear and nuisance of mosquito is called (c) — mosquito menace. For (d) — city dwellers it is (e) — constant nuisance. Particularly at (f) — night, it becomes more when thousands of mosquitoes start singing around (g) — us. Even during daytimes, we are not free from (h) —attack of mosquitoes. To prevent (i) — nuisance caused by mosquitoes, we have to be alert and work in (j) — assorted efforts.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Use "the" at a because a superlative ("most talked-about") requires the definite article: "the most talked-about topics." Use "the" at b and c because they refer to a specific concept already introduced ("the fear... = the mosquito menace"), and use "a" at e because "constant nuisance" is a singular countable noun. No article is needed before general plurals or fixed expressions—so (d) "city dwellers", (f) "at night", (g) "us", and (j) "assorted efforts" take no article—while (h) and (i) use "the" because they refer to a particular attack/nuisance already mentioned.

Question #11 (ID: 209603)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
At present, Bangladesh faces (a) — number of (b) — problems. Of all these problems (c) — population problem is (d) — most acute one. Population is undoubtedly (e) —great asset to (f) — country. But when (g) — country fails to feed and provide them with (h) — basic necessities of life, they become (i) — burden. Similar is (j) — case with Bangladesh.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক ও খ-এ "a large number of social" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে কারণ 'number of' এর আগে পরিমাণ বোঝাতে 'a large' লাগে এবং সমস্যার ধরন জানাতে 'social' সঠিক। গ ও ঘ-এ 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে কারণ নির্দিষ্ট 'population problem' ও 'most acute one' সম্পর্কে বলা হচ্ছে, আর ঙ-এ 'a' দিয়ে 'a great asset' বোঝানো হয়েছে। চ, ছ, জ, ঝ ও ঞ-এ 'the' বা 'a' দেওয়া হয়েছে নির্দিষ্টতা অনুযায়ী: নির্দিষ্ট হলে 'the' (the country, the basic necessities, the case) এবং সাধারণভাবে একক কিছু বোঝাতে 'a' (a burden) ব্যবহৃত হয়।

Question #12 (ID: 209604)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Adnan is a brilliant student. He is (a) — asset. One day he may be (b) — engineer or (c) — doctor. He makes (d) — best use of his time He makes a proper division of his time and does his duties accordingly. He knows that youth is (e) — golden period of (f) — life. He has (g) — aim in life. He knows that life without (h) — aim is like (i) —ship without (j) — rudder.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Use 'an' before vowel sounds and 'a' before consonant sounds, so (a) "an asset", (b) "an engineer", (c) "a doctor", (g) "an aim", (h) "an aim", (i) "a ship" and (j) "a rudder".  
Use 'the' for a specific or unique thing and 'one's' for general possession, so (d) "the best use", (e) "the golden period" and (f) "one's life".

(a) — morning walk is (b) — good habit for all classes of (c) — people. It is (d) — simple exercise and good for health and (e) — mentality. In the morning, (f) — air is fresh and free from any kind of noise and pollution. This pure (g) — environment makes (h) — effect on (i) — nature in (j) — morning.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: একক গণনীয় বস্তুর সাধারণ কোন একটি বোঝাতে অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল 'a/an' লাগে — তাই (a), (b), (d) এ 'a' এবং স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হওয়ায় (h) এ 'an' লাগে। পরিচিত বা নির্দিষ্ট কিছু বোঝাতে 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয় — তাই (f) ও (j) তে 'the' সঠিক। 'this' থাকলে আর্টিকেল লাগে না এবং সাধারণভাবে বা বহুসংখ্যক/অগণনীয় রূপে ব্যবহৃত শব্দগুলোর আগে আর্টিকেল লাগবে না — ফলে (c), (e), (g), (i) এ কোনো আর্টিকেল নেই।

Question #14 (ID: 209606)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A library is (a) — part and parcel of (b) — educational institution. It is (c) — unique place where books of different subjects are kept for (d) — reading. It enables (e) —readers to read books of their choice that creates (f) — enthusiasm for learning. Students should pay (g) — visit to (h) — library regularly. They can borrow books for (i) —certain period and return them after (j) — given time.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: শব্দের ধ্বনি ও সাধারণ নিয়ম অনুসারে—'integral' ও 'educational' স্বরধ্বনি শুরু তাই (a) ও (b) হবে 'an'; 'unique' শব্দটির শুরুতে 'y' ধ্বনি হওয়ায় (c) হবে 'a'. 'reading' ও 'enthusiasm' অব্যক্ত, অগণনীয় ধারণা, তাই (d) ও (f) তে কোনো article লাগে না; সাধারণ বহুবচন হিসেবে 'readers' এ article লাগে না (e = none)। 'pay a visit' একটি স্থায়ী বলবৎ অংশ, তাই (g) 'a'; নির্দিষ্ট স্থানের জন্য (h) হবে 'the library'; নির্দিষ্ট সময় বা সময়সীমার ক্ষেত্রে (i) 'a certain period' এবং (j) 'the given time' যাবে।

Question #15 (ID: 209607)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2013 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Galib works in (a) — nationalized bank in Dhaka, (b) — capital city of Bangladesh. Being (c) — sensitive young man and (d) — ex-student of (e) — English literature, he takes the job as (f) — source of pleasure. As (g) — honest officer, he tries to give his best to (h) — clients. Everyday hundreds of people come to (i) — bank and Galib happens to come across many of them with (j) — smiling face.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
The rule: use [math]'a'[/math] for a non‑specific singular countable noun, [math]'an'[/math] before vowel sounds, [math]'the'[/math] for a specific or unique noun, and no article before academic subjects. Applying this: (a) a nationalized bank (non‑specific), (b) the capital city (unique), (c) a sensitive young man, (d) an ex‑student, (e) English literature (no article), (f) a source of pleasure, (g) an honest officer (silent “h”), (h) the clients and (i) the bank (specific to his workplace), (j) a smiling face (each person has one).

Question #16 (ID: 209608)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Tea is a drink. It is also (a) — refreshing drink. The preparation of tea is a long but (b) — interesting process. (c) — water is first boiled in (d) — kettle and (e) — desired quantity of (f) — tea dust is put in it. After (g) — few minutes (h) — boilled  leaves are separated from (i) — liquor. Then the liquor is poured into (j) — cup and some milk and sugar are mixed with it.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
Explanation: These blanks test article use. Use "a" before consonant sounds ((a) a, (d) a, (j) a) and "an" before vowel sounds ((b) an); use "the" for specific or already‑known items ((c) the, (e) the, (h) the, (i) the); use "a few" for a small number ((g) a); and use no article with the uncountable noun "tea dust" ((f) —, zero article).

Question #17 (ID: 209609)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) ———– 16th December is (b) ———-red letter day in the history of Bangladesh. On this day, we achieved (c) ———- freedom at the cost of (d) ———- bloody battle and Bangladesh came into (e)———-being and made a place in (f)———-world map as (g) ———- independent country. Every year this day is celebrated in (h) ———- enthusiastic atmosphere. We remember (i) ———-great sacrifice of our heroic sons who died for this country. We also pay (j)———-great tribute to them.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
slove add kora lagbe

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: ক এখানে বিশেষ একটি তারিখ নির্দেশ করা হচ্ছে, তাই "the" ব্যবহৃত হবে; খ "red‑letter day" এখানে সাধারণ একটি দিন, তাই অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল "a" লাগে।  
গ আমাদের স্বাধীনতা হওয়ায় মালিকানার শব্দ "our" ব্যবহার করা উচিত; ঘ একক গননাযোগ্য ঘটনা নির্দেশ করলে "a" ব্যবহার করা হয় ("a bloody battle"); ঙ "came into being" একটি স্থির выражение, তাই এখানে অতিরিক্ত আর্টিকেল লাগে না।  
চ "the world map" যখন সারা বিশ্বের একক মানচিত্রকে বোঝায় তখন "the" লাগে; ছ "independent" শুরুর স্বরধ্বনির কারণে "an" ব্যবহৃত হয়; জ একইভাবে "enthusiastic" শব্দের আগে "an" লাগে।  
ঝ জাতির উদ্দেশ্যে করা নির্দিষ্ট ত্যাগকে নির্দেশ করতে "the great sacrifice" উপযুক্ত; ঞ "tribute" একক গণনাযোগ্য হলে "a great tribute" বলা যায় (অথবা সাধারণভাবে "pay great tribute"ও প্রচলিত)।

Question #18 (ID: 209610)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once upon (a) ———-time there was (b) ——— king. His palace was surrounded by (c) ————–beautiful gardens. One day he fell ill. He called in (d)———— doctor. But (e) ———–doctor could not say what wrong was with him. More (f)——— doctors were called. Finally they said that (g)———-king could be healed if he wore (h) ———– shirt of (i) ———– happy man. (j)———-messengers were sent everywhere, but no happy man could be found.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Once upon (a) a time and there was (b) a king because we use the indefinite article "a" to introduce singular countable nouns for the first time. He called in (d) a doctor (introducing one doctor) but (e) the doctor (the same, specific doctor just mentioned) could not help, and (f) more doctors needs no article because "more" quantifies the plural. Finally (g) the king (specific king) could be healed if he wore (h) the shirt of (i) a happy man (any happy man), and (j) many messengers shows a large number sent.

Question #19 (ID: 209611)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Long long ago (a) ——— mirror was found in (b) ———paddy field by (c)———-old farmer. Neither this farmer nor anybody else in (d) ——— area had ever seen a mirror. So, when (e) ———-farmer looked into (f) ——— mirror, he was surprised to see (g)  —— man looking straight at him. Now, (h) ——— farmer closely (i) ———-resembled his father who had died many years ago. He thought that it was his father (j) ——— inside it and saluted him with love and respect.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Most blanks are articles: a is used for first mention of a singular countable noun (a mirror, a paddy field), c is an before a vowel sound ("an old farmer"), and d, e, f, h take the because they refer to specific things or people already known; g is a for an indefinite "man." The blank i needs no extra word because "closely resembled" is already complete, and j is filled by "who was" to form the relative clause "he thought that it was his father who was inside it."

Question #20 (ID: 209612)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Socrates believed that (a) ——-angry man was more of (b)———-beast than human being. He had a wife who used to lose her temper on (c) ———-slightest excuse. One day (d) ———-woman got more furious and began to insult him. He went out and sat on the door step of his (e) ———house. He looked out on the public (f)——- street. The wife found that he was paying (g) ——— least heed to her. So she began to pour hot water on (h) ——-head of Socrates. The passers-by were very amused at (i) ———– incident. They had seen such (j) ——- incident before.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Answers: (a) an, (b) a, (c) the, (d) the, (e) own, (f) the, (g) the, (h) his, (i) the, (j) an. Explanation: Use [math]an[/math] before a vowel sound ("angry") and [math]a[/math] before a consonant sound ("beast"); [math]the[/math] marks something definite or already mentioned ("the slightest excuse," "the woman," "the public street," "the incident," and the fixed phrase "the least heed"); use possessives ([math]own[/math], [math]his[/math]) for belonging; and [math]such\ an[/math] is required before a vowel-starting noun ("incident").

Question #21 (ID: 209613)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Childhood or boyhood is (a) ———-man’s formative period. During this period (b) ——– child receives training from its mother, (c) ———-mother’s tender heart always looks to (d) ———-welfare and well-being of (e) ———child. If during this period (f) ———  mother tries to bring (g) ———–child up carefully and according to her (h)———-best ideas, (i) ——child is sure to grow with its superiors, parents and teachers and love (j) ——— all irrespective of cast creed and colour.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: (a) "a" — use the indefinite article for "a man" in a general statement; (b) "the" — the child in that specific formative period is definite; (c) "whose" — relative pronoun showing the mother’s possession of the tender heart; (d) "the" and (e) "the" — "the welfare" and "the child" are definite and already identified; (f), (g), (i) "the" — same definite "mother" and "child" already mentioned; (h) "own" — "her own best ideas" emphasizes possession; (j) "one and all" — the idiom meaning everybody irrespective of caste, creed or colour.

Question:
Today women are playing (a) ——- important role in all spheres of (b) ——- life. They are no longer confined within (c)———– four walls of the kitchens. They have come out of their cocoons and are working hand in hand with (d)———-men. They are joining (e) ———– wide range of professions and making a great (f)———– contribution to the economy. Now it has come to (g)——realisation of all that it is not possible to develop the country keeping women, (h) —– large section of (i) —– population, in (j)——-dark.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সঠিক শব্দগুলো হলো — ক 'an' (ভোক্ত ধ্বনিতে শুরু হওয়া 'important'–এর আগে 'an' লাগে), খ 'public' ('spheres of public life' বাংলা-বাক্যে প্রচলিত collocation), গ 'the' ('the four walls' নির্দিষ্ট স্থান নির্দেশ করে), ঘ 'men' ('with men' সরাসরি বহুবচন), ঙ 'a' ('a wide range' idiomatic), চ 'financial' ('financial contribution' অর্থগত অবদান বোঝায়), ছ 'the' ('come to the realisation'–এ 'the realisation' স্বভাবতই নির্দিষ্ট), জ 'a' ('a large section' অনির্দিষ্ট অংশ বোঝায়), ঝ 'the' ('of the population'–এ নির্দিষ্ট জনসংখ্যা), ঞ 'the' ('in the dark' একটি idiomatic phrase)।

Question #23 (ID: 209615)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2012 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) ———- ant is (b)———- industrious insect. Bees are also (c) —– industrious insects. If we observe the life of (d)———-successful man, we will find that he is also (e) ———-industrious, (f)———-industrious are appreciated by all. On the other hand, (g) —–idle are disliked by all. So, industry is (h) ———-must to prosper in (i) ———- life. We all know that industry is the key to success and laziness leads us to (j)———-misfortune.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
The answers use correct articles and common collocations: use an before the vowel sound in "ant" and a before "successful man"; very strengthens the adjective "industrious"; the before an adjective (the industrious, the idle) turns it into a group noun. Also, "a must" is the idiomatic expression for necessity, "one's life" shows possession, and "certain misfortune" is the natural collocation meaning an inevitable bad result.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Bangladesh is (a) ———world’s most densely populated country. Our development efforts are frustrated because of (b) —–great size of our population, (c)____population explosion is (d)-______constant threat to our environment and (e)- society. Her population is growing at such (f)____high rate that (g)_______environment may soon fail to supply (h)— —– people with their minimum necessities. It is indeed (i) ——–alarming situation. Something should be done to change (j)————situation.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: 'the' নির্দিষ্ট বা একমাত্র বস্তু নির্দেশ করতে ব্যবহৃত হয় (অতএব (a), (b), (c), (g), (h) এ 'the'), 'a' সাধারণ/অস্পষ্ট একক বস্তু বোঝায় (এখানে (d) ও (f) এ), 'an' স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হওয়া শব্দের আগে লাগে ((i) এ), 'to' লাগে 'threat to' collocation-এ ((e) এ), এবং বর্তমানে থাকা পরিস্থিতি দেখাতে 'this' ব্যবহার করা হয় ((j) এ)। তাই সঠিক শব্দগুলো হলো: (a) the, (b) the, (c) the, (d) a, (e) to, (f) a, (g) the, (h) the, (i) an, (j) this.

Question #25 (ID: 209544)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a)— honest boy is he who never tells a lie, He carries out (b)———– orders of his parents. He has (c)———aim in life. He develops (d) ———attitude to serve his nation. He is (e)——— active worker who upholds (f)——— interest of his nation above everything. He thinks that he has (g)———role to play in all matters. We cordially expect such (h)——- boy to change (i) -—– selfish motive of (j)—–people.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use "an" before words beginning with a vowel sound — hence "An honest", "an aim", "an attitude", "an active". Use "the" for things made specific or definite — "the orders of his parents", "the interest of his nation", "the selfish motive of the people". Use "a" before a consonant sound — "a role", and the fixed phrase "such a boy".

Question #26 (ID: 209545)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There was (a)_idle man who inherited vast property from his father. He did not like physical labour. As (b) _ _ result, he became very fat and could not move from one place to another. He called in (c)_European doctor, (d)_doctor was very intelligent. He did not prescribe any medicine for (e)_man. He advised him to buy (f)_heavy club and move it in (g) __ air till he got (h)_tired. Following the advice of the doctor, he became (i)_thin from (j)_obese man.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use articles and set phrases correctly: (a) and (j) take "an" because "idle" and "obese" begin with vowel sounds; (c) and (f) take "a" because "European" (y‑sound) and "heavy" begin with consonant sounds. Use "the" for specific, already mentioned people ((d) the doctor, (e) the man). (b) is the fixed phrase "as a result", (g) is "the air" in this context, (h) is the adjective "tired" (no article), and (i) is the adjective "thin" describing the result.

Question #28 (ID: 209547)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
At present Bangladesh faces (a) _____ number of (b) ____ problems. Of all these problems (c) ____ population problem is (d) _____ most acute one. Population is undoubtedly (e)______great asset of (f)_____country. But when (g)_____country fails to feed and provide them with (h) ______ suitable jobs, they become (i) _____ burden. Similar is (j)____case with Bangladesh.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) "a large" and (b) "serious" — "a large number of" is the common phrase for many, and "serious" describes the kind of problems.  
(c) "the" and (d) "the" — we use "the population problem" and "the most acute" because we mean a specific problem among those mentioned.  
(e) "a" and (f) "the" — "a great asset" is the correct indefinite phrase, while "the country" refers to Bangladesh already identified.  
(g) "the", (h) "any" and (i) "a" — "the country" (specific), "any suitable jobs" shows absence of jobs, and "a burden" is the correct indefinite noun phrase.  
(j) "the" — "the case" is the fixed expression meaning the situation is the same for Bangladesh.

Question #29 (ID: 209548)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
I live in (a)_____Jigatola near (b)_____Rifles Square. When I was (c) _____ student of  (d)_____University of Dhaka, I stayed at Wari in (e)_____old Dhaka. Actually, it was in (f)______Bonogram Lane that originates from (g)______BCC Road which is a branch of (h)______Renkin Street, (i)______Bangabhaban and (j)_____ Baldha Garden are adjacent to this area.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Use no article before most proper place names: names like Jigatola, Rifles Square, Bonogram Lane, BCC Road, Renkin Street, Bangabhaban and Baldha Garden are specific names, so they normally take no article. Use "a" for a single, countable noun ("a student") and "the" before a specific institution name ("the University of Dhaka").

Question #30 (ID: 209549)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
We live on (a)______ground floor of (b)_____old house on (c)______river Kirtankhola. We are very much afraid of (d) ______ burglars and always lock up (e)______house very carefully before we go to (f) ______bed. We also take (g)_____ precaution of looking under (h)_____bed to see if (i)_____burglar is hiding there. We know modern burglars do not hide under beds, but we go on looking just (j)____same.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা: সাধারণ নিয়ম হলো — ক প্রকারের ক্ষেত্রে 'the' ব্যবহার করি যখন কিছু নির্দিষ্ট বা পরিচিত বোঝাতে হয়, 'an' ব্যবহার হয় স্বরধ্বনিতে শুরু করা অচিহ্নিত একক নাউনের আগে, কোনো আর্টিকেল না থাকে (zero article) যখন সার্বজনীন বহুবচন বা স্বরূপ অভিব্যক্তি লাগে (যেমন "go to bed" বা "afraid of burglars"), এবং 'a' ব্যবহার হয় অনির্দিষ্ট একক করে কাউন্টেবল নামের আগে; "the same" একটি স্থায়ী ফ্রেজ। নিচে প্রতিটি খালি স্থানের উত্তর ও সংক্ষিপ্ত কারণ আছে:

ক the — "ground floor" এখানে বিশেষভাবে আমাদের ঘরের মেঝে বলছে, তাই নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল।  
খ an — "old" শব্দটি স্বরধ্বনিতে শুরু হওয়ায় অনির্দিষ্ট এককের জন্য 'an'।  
গ the — নদীর নাম হওয়ায় (River Kirtankhola) 'the' লাগে।  
ঘ (শূন্য আর্টিকেল) — "burglars" বহুবচনভাবে সাধারণ ধরন বোঝায়, তাই কোনো আর্টিকেল দরকার নেই।  
ঙ the — এখানে নির্দিষ্ট আমাদের ঘরকে বোঝাচ্ছে, তাই 'the house'।  
চ (শূন্য আর্টিকেল) — ইংরেজিতে "go to bed" বলার সময় আর্টিকেল ব্যবহার করা হয় না।  
ছ the — নির্দিষ্ট সেই সাবধানতা (the precaution) বোঝাতে 'the' ভালো মানায়।  
জ the — একই কারণে নির্দিষ্ট বেডের নিচে, 'the bed'।  
ঝ a — এখানে কোনো অজ্ঞাত এক ব্যক্তি (a burglar), তাই 'a'।  
ঞ the — "just the same" একটি স্থায়ী идиম, তাই 'the same'।

Question #31 (ID: 209550)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
You must have heard (a)_____name of Kazi Nazrul Islam. He is our national poet. He is known as (b)_____rebel poet. He was born in (c)_____poor family. He passed his boyhood in great hardship. When (d) _____ First World War .broke out, he joined (e) ______army. After (f)______war, he began to write poems. He wrote specially for (g) ______ oppressed and down trodden people. He is called (h) _______ Shelley of Bengali literature. His poems and songs inspired (i) _______ Bangalees in (j) _______ War of liberation.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Use "the" for (a), (b), (d), (e), (f), (g), (h), (i) and (j) because they refer to a specific or definite thing (the name, the recognised title "Rebel Poet", the First World War, the army he joined, that war, the oppressed as a definite group, the Shelley comparison, the Bangalees and the War of Liberation). Use "a" for (c) because "born in a poor family" refers to one nonspecific family among many. Thus: (a) the; (b) the; (c) a; (d) the; (e) the; (f) the; (g) the; (h) the; (i) the; (j) the.

Question #32 (ID: 209551)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards: Dhaka Board | Tags: Dhaka Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
(a) ————— Morning walk is a good habit for all classes of people. It is (b) ———simple exercise and good for health and (c)———–mentality. In the morning, (d) ———- air is fresh and free from any kind of noise and pollution. This pure (e) –— environment makes an effect on (i)———–walkers’ health and mind, when (g)——-— man enjoys (h)—— – beauties and solemnity of (i) ———nature in (j)———– morning.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
(a) "A", (b) "a", (c) "sound", (d) "the", (e) "healthy", (f) "the" (before walkers), (g) "a", (h) "the", (i) "nature", (j) "the".  
These choices follow article and adjective rules: use "a"/"A" for a single, non‑specific item ((a),(b),(g)); use "the" for specific things or fixed expressions ((d),(f),(h),(j)); "sound" and "healthy" are adjectives describing "mentality" and "environment"; and "nature" is usually used without an article when spoken of in general.

Question #33 (ID: 209552)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
It is (a)————known fact that English is (b)————-international language. (c).—— language used by international community is important. Statistics show that 350 million people speak English as (d)—–—— first language and another 300 million use it as (e)———— second, language. It is (f)——-official language in more than 60 countries of the world. Once it was also (g)————official language of our country. Most of (h)———– books of science and technology are written in English, So (i)———– importance of learning English beggars description. It is (j)———must.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation:
a "a well-known" is needed because we use an article + adjective before "known fact". b "an" is used before the vowel sound in "international". c "the" refers to that particular language used by the international community.

d "their" shows possession for the people whose first language it is. e "a" fits the phrase "a second language". f "an" indicates one of the official languages in many countries. g "the" refers to the specific former official language of our country.

h "the" points to that particular group of books. i "its" shows possession ("its importance"). j "a" completes the idiom "a must".

Question #34 (ID: 209553)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards: Rajshahi Board | Tags: Rajshahi Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Though newspaper is not always (a)———— unmixed blessing, it is (b) —————-most useful thing in our life. We rarely think of (c) ————-day without reading (d) ———-, newspaper. Reading newspaper is one of (e) —-——good habits of a man. We shall be like (f)———— frog in a dark well if we neglect developing this habit. However, some people prefer (g)————electronic media to reading (h) ——————- newspaper. But (i) ————newspaper offers more to its readers than (j)—————electronic media.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use articles and omission of articles according to sound, specificity and countability. (a) takes "an" because "unmixed" begins with a vowel sound; (b) takes "the" because we use "the" with superlatives ("the most useful"); (c), (d) and (f) take "a" because they refer to a non‑specific singular ("a day," "a newspaper," "a frog"); (e) needs "the" in "one of the best habits" since "best" is a superlative; (g) and (j) have no article because "electronic media" is treated as a plural/uncountable noun; (i) takes "the" when referring to the newspaper as a specific medium that offers more than electronic media.

Question #35 (ID: 209554)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once you have completed (a)———-initial diagnosis of your students, you are faced with selecting subject-matter appropriate to their (b)———-interests, abilities, and personal – social adjustment as well as to your own teaching objectives. Frequently, (c) ————– selection and planning of content are not seen as integral (d)———-parts of (e) ———- evaluation process, (f) ———– techniques you select to evaluate how well you and your students have achieved your objectives are inextricably bound to (g)———– subject-matter used to teach these objectives. In (h) ———-sense, you must evaluate (i)——— subject-matter itself to (j) ———-determine if it is appropriate for your objectives.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:

Use "the" with "selection and planning" and with "evaluation process" and "techniques" because these refer to specific, definite items in the teaching context. Use "this" in "in this sense" to point back to the previous idea, and the infinitive "to determine" shows the purpose of evaluating the subject-matter.

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board

Question:
Providing enough energy to meet (a) ————ever-increasing demand is one of (b)———— gravest problems (c)----—world is now facing. Energy is (d)———— key to (e) ——– industrialized economy, which calls for (f)———– doubling of electrical output every ten to twelve years. Meanwhile (g) ———– days of cheap abundant and environmentally acceptable power may be coming to (h)———end. Coal is plentiful but polluting, natural gas is (i)———–scarce, oil is not found everywhere. Nuclear power now appears (j)————-costly and risky.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Correct answers: (a) the, (b) the, (c) the, (d) the, (e) an, (f) a, (g) the, (h) an, (i) scarce, (j) to be.

Question #37 (ID: 209556)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Cellular radio telephone, also called cellular telephone or cell phone provides voice telephone and other services to (a)———–mobile users. Cellular telephones primarily operate like portable or cordless telephones. However, unlike conventional wire-based cordless phones, cell phones are completely portable and do not require (b) ————jack to access (c) ————-wire-based networks operated by local telephone companies, (d)————– new generation of services for cell phones include video conferencing and (e)——– internet access with (f) ———— ability to send e-mail. Cellular telephones have become very popular with (g) —————professionals and (h)———-consumers as (i)———–way to communicate easily. It has been (j)————–alternative to conventional wire-based services.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
The correct answers emphasize that cell phones serve users “on the move” and do not require a physical telephone jack because cellular systems use radio links to connect handsets to base stations and the local wire network. Newer generations provide video conferencing and mobile Internet with the ability to send e‑mail because modern cellular networks support higher data rates and packet‑switched services for multimedia. For these reasons cell phones are popular with busy professionals and ordinary consumers as a convenient, portable and viable alternative to conventional wire‑based telephone service.

Newspaper plays (a) ———important role in our society. It is (b)——–most useful thing in our modern life. We cannot think of (c)——–day without it. --------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
When (a) ———— great poet, Ferdousi, began to write (b).—— Shahnama, the sultan promised him (c) ————piece of gold for each (d)   ———-verse. When (e) ——– epic was finished, it contained sixty thousand (f) ———— verses. Instead of giving gold coins, he offered the poet only sixty thousand silver (g) ————- coins. The poet refused to take the silver coins and left the court with (h)——--broken heart. He was (i)—–---aggrieved man. Later on the sultan realised that he had made (j)——blunder.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:

So the answers are: (a) the, (b) the, (c) a, (d) (no article), (e) the, (f) (no article), (g) (no article), (h) a, (i) an, (j) a — because "the great poet" and "the Shahnama" are specific, "a piece" is any single piece, "each" and "sixty thousand" take no article, and "an" precedes a vowel sound in "aggrieved."

Question #46 (ID: 209565)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
An angry man is not liked (a) ——--- even by (b) ——--- idiot. There is difference between the educated and (c) –----- uneducated. An educated (d) ——---  person should come forward to educate (e)—— uneducated. On the other hand (f)–rich man should have (g) ——---  sympathy for (h) ——--- poor there is difference between (i)——-- poor man and (j) ——--- rich man.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Use [math]"by"[/math] because the clause is passive ("liked by even an idiot") and [math]"an"[/math] before a vowel sound ("an idiot"). Use [math]"the"[/math] to talk about definite groups ("the educated and the uneducated", "the poor", "the rich"), omit any extra word between "educated" and "person" ("An educated person"), and use [math]"some"[/math] for an indefinite amount of sympathy. So the blanks are: (a) by, (b) an, (c) the, (d) — (no word), (e) the, (f) the, (g) some, (h) the, (i) the, (j) the.

Question #47 (ID: 209566)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board

Question:
We were returning home. On (a)——–way we met (b) ———little girl. She was selling (c) —— flowers on (d) ———street. She requested us to buy (e)——–flower. My mother is (f)——–kind-hearted woman, (g)——–motherly affection rose at (h)——— sight of her. She gave her (i) ——— ten taka note and bought some flowers. We should be kind to (j) —--— helpless.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Answers: (a) our, (b) a, (c) some, (d) the, (e) a, (f) a, (g) her, (h) the, (i) a, (j) the helpless.

These fit because "our" shows whose way it was; "a" is the indefinite article for a singular noun ("a little girl", "a flower", "a ten taka note"); "some" is used for an indefinite plural ("some flowers"); "the" is used for a specific or familiar noun ("the street", the fixed phrase "the sight"); "her" shows the mother's possession of the affection; and "the helpless" uses "the" to refer to a particular group (people who are helpless).

Question:
There was (a)_idle man who inherited vast property from his father. He did not like physical labour. As (b) _ _ result, he became very fat and could not move from one place to another. He called in (c)_European doctor, (d)_doctor was very intelligent. He did not prescribe any medicine for (e)_man. He advised him to buy (f)_heavy club and move it in (g) __ air till he got (h)_tired. Following the advice of the doctor, he became (i)_thin from (j)_obese man.

Options:


Correct Answer:

Explanation:

"As a result" is a fixed phrase for (b); (c) = "a European doctor" because "European" begins with a consonant sound (/j/); (d) and (e) = "the" to refer back to the specific doctor and man; (f) = "a heavy club" (nonspecific); (g) = "the air" (the specific medium); (h) and (i) need no article ("till he got tired," "he became thin").

Question #51 (ID: 209570)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
“Under the Greenwood Tree” is (a)____song derived from “As Your Like It,” (b) ____ comedy by  Shakespeare. In this song (c)_____writer’s love of nature has found (d)______ eloquent expression, as has, as (e) ______ undertone, his deep concern for (f)_____ limitations of (g)______human society. In the forest (h)______only enemy of man is bitter winter and rough weather. Nature has no particular enmity towards man and it treats undoubtedly (e)_____great asset of (f)______country. But when (g) _____ country fails to feed and provide them with (h) ____suitable jobs, they become (i) ____ burden. Similar is (j)_____case with Bangladesh.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Use of articles: (a) and (b) take "a" because they name one non‑specific item ("a song", "a comedy"), while "an" is used before the vowel sound in "an undertone." Use "the" for specific references—e.g. "the writer", "the limitations", "the only enemy", and "the country" when a particular entity is meant. Omit an article in idiomatic or general expressions: "found eloquent expression" (no article) and "human society" when speaking generally.

Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
- ক "a large" ও খ "serious" — কারণ ইংরেজিতে "a large number of" একটি idiom যে অনেক কিছুকে বোঝায় এবং "serious" সমস্যাগুলোর চরিত্র বর্ণনা করে।  
- গ "the" ও ঘ "the" — নির্দিষ্ট সব সমস্যার মধ্যে জনসংখ্যা সমস্যা আলাদা ও নির্দিষ্ট হওয়ায় 'the' লাগে।  
- ঙ "a" ও চ "the" — "a great asset" অনির্দিষ্ট একটি গুণ বা সম্পদ বোঝায়, আর "of the country"–এ দেশটি নির্দিষ্ট তাই 'the' ব্যবহার করি।  
- ছ "the", জ "any" ও ঝ "a" — দেশের ব্যর্থতা নির্দিষ্ট হওয়ায় 'the country', নেতিবাচক প্রসঙ্গে 'any suitable jobs' প্রযোজ্য, এবং তারা হলে 'a burden' সাধারণ ধারণা প্রকাশ করে।  
- ঞ "the" — ইংরেজিতে "the case" একটি স্থায়ী idiom, তাই 'the' প্রয়োজন।

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board

Question:
I live in (a)_____Jigatola near (b)_____Rifles Square. When I was (c) _____ student of  (d)_____University of Dhaka, I stayed at Wari in (e)_____old Dhaka. Actually, it was in (f)______Bonogram Lane that originates from (g)______BCC Road which is a branch of (h)______Renkin Street, (i)______Bangabhaban and (j)_____ Baldha Garden are adjacent to this area.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
ব্যাখ্যা:
ক Jigatola একটি স্থানের বিশেষ নাম, তাই আর্টিকেল লাগে না।  
খ Rifles Square নাম হতো; সাধারণত নামের আগে আর্টিকেল প্রয়োজন হয় না।  
গ a — 'student' here is indefinite (একজন ছাত্র), তাই 'a' হয়।  
ঘ the — 'University of Dhaka' একটি নির্দিষ্ট প্রতিষ্ঠান, তাই 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয়।  
ঙ Old Dhaka একটি স্থান-নাম (Old Dhaka), আর্টিকেল ছাড়া।  
চ Bonogram Lane রাসের নাম, আর্টিকেল লাগে না।  
ছ BCC Road রাসের নাম, আর্টিকেল ছাড়া।  
জ Renkin Street রাসের নাম—আর্টিকেল লাগেনা।  
ঝ Bangabhaban প্রতিষ্ঠিত নাম (প্রেসিডেনশিয়াল প্যালেস), সাধারণভাবে আর্টিকেল ছাড়া।  
ঞ Baldha Garden উদ্যানের নাম, তাই আর্টিকেল ব্যবহার করা হয় না।

Question #54 (ID: 209573)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2011 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
We live on (a)______ground floor of (b)_____old house on (c)______river Kirtankhola. We are very much afraid of (d) ______ burglars and always lock up (e)______house very carefully before we go to (f) ______bed. We also take (g)_____ precaution of looking under (h)_____bed to see if (i)_____burglar is hiding there. We know modern burglars do not hide under beds, but we go on looking just (j)____same.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Use "the" for specific, known things (we mean our ground floor, the river Kirtankhola, our house and our bed), and in the fixed phrase "just the same." Use "an" before a singular noun beginning with a vowel sound ("an old house"). Omit the article for general plurals ("burglars") and in the idiom "go to bed"; use "the precaution" in the set phrase "take the precaution of..." and "a burglar" for an unspecified single intruder.

Question #57 (ID: 209576)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
It is (a)————known fact that English is (b)————-international language. (c).—— language used by international community is important. Statistics show that 350 million people speak English as (d)—–—— first language and another 300 million use it as (e)———— second, language. It is (f)——-official language in more than 60 countries of the world. Once it was also (g)————official language of our country. Most of (h)———– books of science and technology are written in English, So (i)———– importance of learning English beggars description. It is (j)———must.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Answers: (a) a well-known, (b) an, (c) the, (d) their, (e) a, (f) an, (g) the, (h) the, (i) its, (j) a.

Explanation: "A well-known" is the correct adjective phrase; use "an" before the vowel sound in "international" and "an" before "official" when non-specific. "The" points to a specific thing already referred to; "their" shows people's first language, while "its" shows possession for English; "a" before "second language" and "a must" are standard idioms.

Question:
Though newspaper is not always (a)———— unmixed blessing, it is (b) —————-most useful thing in our life. We rarely think of (c) ————-day without reading (d) ———-, newspaper. Reading newspaper is one of (e) —-——good habits of a man. We shall be like (f)———— frog in a dark well if we neglect developing this habit. However, some people prefer (g)————electronic media to reading (h) ——————- newspaper. But (i) ————newspaper offers more to its readers than (j)—————electronic media.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: 
(a) "an" — used before a vowel sound in "unmixed." 
(b) "one of the" — shows the newspaper is among the most useful things. 
(c) "a" — "a day" = any single day (indefinite). 
(d) "the" — refers to the newspaper we habitually read (definite). 
(e) "the" — in the phrase "one of the good habits" we use "the." 
(f) "a" — "a frog" is an indefinite singular. 
(g) no article (or just "electronic media") — used generally without "the." 
(h) "the" — again the specific newspaper being read. 
(i) "the" — "the newspaper" as a specific medium. 
(j) no article ("electronic media") — used in general (compare: the newspaper offers more than electronic media).

Question #59 (ID: 209578)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards:  | Tags: Jessore Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once you have completed (a)———-initial diagnosis of your students, you are faced with selecting subject-matter appropriate to their (b)———-interests, abilities, and personal – social adjustment as well as to your own teaching objectives. Frequently, (c) ————– selection and planning of content are not seen as integral (d)———-parts of (e) ———- evaluation process, (f) ———– techniques you select to evaluate how well you and your students have achieved your objectives are inextricably bound to (g)———– subject-matter used to teach these objectives. In (h) ———-sense, you must evaluate (i)——— subject-matter itself to (j) ———-determine if it is appropriate for your objectives.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
"an" is correct for (a) because "initial" begins with a vowel sound and takes an indefinite article; "varying" fits (b) since it describes differences in students' interests, abilities, and adjustment.  
"The" is appropriate for (c), (e), (f), and (g) because these nouns (the selection, the evaluation process, the techniques, the subject-matter) are specific and definite; "integral parts" needs no extra word between "integral" and "parts."  
"This" in (h) is idiomatic ("in this sense"), "the" in (i) specifies the particular subject-matter to be assessed, and "to determine" in (j) correctly expresses the purpose of the evaluation.

Meanwhile (g) ———– days of cheap abundant and environmentally acceptable power may be coming to (h)———end. Coal is plentiful but polluting, natural gas is (i)———–scarce, oil is not found everywhere. Explanation:

Question #61 (ID: 209580)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2010 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Cellular radio telephone, also called cellular telephone or cell phone provides voice telephone and other services to (a)———–mobile users. Cellular telephones primarily operate like portable or cordless telephones. However, unlike conventional wire-based cordless phones, cell phones are completely portable and do not require (b) ————jack to access (c) ————-wire-based networks operated by local telephone companies, (d)————– new generation of services for cell phones include video conferencing and (e)——– internet access with (f) ———— ability to send e-mail. Cellular telephones have become very popular with (g) —————professionals and (h)———-consumers as (i)———–way to communicate easily. It has been (j)————–alternative to conventional wire-based services.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Correct answers (in context): (a) many, (b) a telephone, (c) the, (d) The, (e) wireless, (f) the, (g) business, (h) ordinary, (i) an easy, (j) a viable.  
Explanation: "many" fits because cell phones serve large numbers of mobile users; "a telephone jack" and "the wire-based networks" fit logically since wired phones need a physical jack to reach local networks. "The new generation" properly introduces newer services, and "wireless internet access with the ability to send e‑mail" describes those features. Finally, "business professionals and ordinary consumers" names typical users, "an easy way" explains the communication purpose, and "a viable alternative" indicates cell phones serve as a practical substitute for wired service.

Solution:

For this reason, (e) ——-tourism business can flourish here, (f) ——-wild animals of (g) ——-Sundarbans are also (h) ——-great asset. Tourism can play (i) ——-vital role in national economy. Question #68 (ID: 209587)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Sylhet Board | Tags: Sylhet Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Newspaper plays (a) ———important role in our society. It is (b)——–most useful thing in our modern life. We cannot think of (c)——–day without it. To read news paper is (d) ——– good habit, (e) ——– more we read newspaper (f) ——– more we can acquire knowledge. If we don’t read it, we shall be (g) ——–frogs in (h) ——–dark well. It is (i) ——–looking glass of (j)——–modern world.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use (a) "an" because "important" begins with a vowel sound; (b) "the" because superlatives like "most useful" take "the". (c) and (d) take "a" for nonspecific singular nouns ("a day", "a good habit"); (e) and (f) are both "the" for the correlative comparative form "the more... the more". Finally, (g) is "like" to show similarity, (h) is "a" before "dark well", and (i) and (j) are "the" because the phrase refers to a specific, definite idea.

Question #69 (ID: 209588)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
When (a) ———— great poet, Ferdousi, began to write (b).—— Shahnama, the sultan promised him (c) ————piece of gold for each (d)   ———-verse. When (e) ——– epic was finished, it contained sixty thousand (f) ———— verses. Instead of giving gold coins, he offered the poet only sixty thousand silver (g) ————- coins. The poet refused to take the silver coins and left the court with (h)——--broken heart. He was (i)—–---aggrieved man. Later on the sultan realised that he had made (j)——blunder.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation: Use "the" for specific, known items—so (a) the (great poet) and (b) the (Shahnama), and (e) the (epic). Use "a" for a single unspecified item—so (c) a (piece of gold), (h) a (broken heart) and (j) a (blunder); use "an" before a vowel sound—so (i) an (aggrieved man). Do not use an article before a singular noun after "each" (so no article before (d) verse) or before plurals after numbers (so no article before (f) verses and (g) coins).

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Chittagong Board | Tags: Chattogram Board

Question:
An angry man is not liked (a) ——--- even by (b) ——--- idiot. There is difference between the educated and (c) –----- uneducated. An educated (d) ——---  person should come forward to educate (e)—— uneducated. On the other hand (f)–rich man should have (g) ——---  sympathy for (h) ——--- poor there is difference between (i)——-- poor man and (j) ——--- rich man.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
Explanation:
a by, b an, c the, d (no word), e the, f a, g some, h the, i a, j a.  
Reason: use [math]by[/math] to show the agent in a passive sentence; use [math]an[/math] before a vowel sound; use [math]the[/math] when referring to a whole class (the educated/the uneducated/the poor); [math]some[/math] works with the uncountable noun sympathy; and [math]a[/math] is for a single, indefinite person.

Question #71 (ID: 209590)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2009 | Boards: Dinajpur Board | Tags: Dinajpur Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
We were returning home. On (a)——–way we met (b) ———little girl. She was selling (c) —— flowers on (d) ———street. She requested us to buy (e)——–flower. My mother is (f)——–kind-hearted woman, (g)——–motherly affection rose at (h)——— sight of her. She gave her (i) ——— ten taka note and bought some flowers. We should be kind to (j) —--— helpless.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:


Explanation:
On (a) "the" is used because "on the way" is a fixed, definite phrase; (b) "a" and (e) "a" and (f) "a" and (i) "a" are indefinite articles before nonspecific singular count nouns ("a little girl", "a flower", "a kind-hearted woman", "a ten-taka note"). (c) "some" is used for an indefinite plural quantity of flowers, (d) "the" fits the common phrase "on the street", (g) "and" joins the clauses, (h) "the" is required in the fixed expression "at the sight of", and (j) "the" makes "the helpless" a general group (people who are helpless).

Question #72 (ID: 209591)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards: Barisal Board | Tags: Barisal Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Truthfulness is (a) — greatest of all (b) — virtues which makes (c) — person really we do not cultivate (d) — habit of speaking (e) — truth, we cannot command (f) — trust of others. The man whom nobody believes can never be famous in life. It may be that we must once or twice by telling (g) — lie but it never brings about (h) — good result. A lien hidden Today or tomorrow it comes to light. Then (i) — real character of (j) — liar is revealed and nobody believes him.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) the (b) x/ the (c) a (d) the (e) the (f) the (g) a (h) a (i) the (j) a

Explanation:
উত্তর: (a) the; (b) — (omit); (c) a; (d) If; (e) the; (f) the; (g) a; (h) a; (i) the; (j) the.

ব্যাখ্যা: 'the' লাগে সর্বোত্তম (superlative) ও নির্দিষ্ট বস্তু বোঝাতে, 'a' লাগে একবচন গণনাযোগ্য নামের আগে, এবং শর্তবোধক বাক্যে 'If' প্রয়োজন—এগুলোই বাক্যের গ্রাম্যাটিকাল সঠিক ব্যবহার নিশ্চিত করে।

Question #73 (ID: 209592)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years: 2017 | Boards:  | Tags: Cumilla Board
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In (a) — last 25 years (b) — world has lost one-third of its natural wealth, according to (c) — International Conservation Organization world wild fund. (d) — earth’s forest, wetlands, seas and coasts are in (e) — worse state today than they were before. Forests are cut down. Moreover, they are being burnt indiscriminately resulting in (f) — increase in carbon-di-oxide and ultimately  (g) — water level is rising as a consequence of global warming. It is anticipated that (h) — new century will face (i) — overwhelming environmental (j) — catastrophe.

Options:


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
(a) the (b) the (c) the (d) The (e) a (f) an (g) the/ × (h) the (i) an (j) ×

Explanation:
Explanation: Use the definite article "the" for specific or unique things — e.g. "the last 25 years," "the world," "the International Conservation Organization," "the earth’s forests," and "the water level." Use the indefinite article "a" before a singular countable noun with a consonant sound ("a worse state") and "an" before a word with a vowel sound ("an increase," "an overwhelming environmental catastrophe"). Also pluralize "forest" to "forests" because multiple types/areas are meant.

Question #74 (ID: 507201)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The community theatre is preparing for its next season. The director wrote a short note: "We are staging (a) — annual play this spring. Because funds are limited, it will not be (b) — easy production. Each actor must learn (c) — scenes well. From (d) — very beginning everyone should be punctual."

Options:
ক. (a) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
খ. (b) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
গ. (c) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন article/pronounটি উপযুক্ত?
ঘ. (d) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "an"
- কারণ: অনেক ইংরেজি শব্দের মধ্যে "annual" শব্দটি স্বরবর্ণ-শব্দ (vowel sound) দিয়ে শুরু করে (এখানে 'a' না বলে 'an' ব্যবহার করতে হয়)।

খ উত্তর: "an"
- কারণ: এখানে "easy production" একটি singular noun phrase; "easy" শব্দটি স্বরবর্ণ-শব্দের মতো মনে হলেও ব্যবহারের নিয়ম অনুযায়ী singular countable noun-এর আগে "an" লাগে ("an easy production") এবং বাক্যে বিরোধী অর্থে ব্যবহার করলেও আর্টিকেল অপরিবর্তিত থাকে: "it will not be an easy production." 

গ উত্তর: "the"
- কারণ: "the scenes" এখানে নির্দিষ্ট দৃশ্যগুলোকে নির্দেশ করে (production-এর নির্দিষ্ট scenes), তাই নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল "the" ব্যবহার করা উচিত।

ঘ উত্তর: "the"
- কারণ: ইংরেজিতে স্থায়ী অভিব্যক্তি "from the very beginning" প্রচলিত; এখানে "the" প্রয়োজন কারণ "very beginning" একটি নির্দিষ্ট সময়কাল নির্দেশ করে।

Explanation:
প্রতিটি নির্বাচন English article/use-এর সাধারণ নিয়ম মেনে করা হয়েছে: (ক) এবং (খ)-এ শব্দগুলি স্বরবর্ণ-শব্দের সাথে শুরু হওয়ায় "an" ব্যবহার উপযোগী; (গ)-এ নির্দিষ্ট সীনের কথা বলা হয়েছে তাই "the" লাগে; (ঘ)-এও স্থায়ী ফ্রেজ "from the very beginning" এ নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল প্রয়োজন।

Question #75 (ID: 507202)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A short travel advisory reads: "Every traveller should carry (a) — umbrella during monsoon. Many people take (b) — unnecessary luggage and regret it later. It is wiser to pack (c) — few essentials than too many items. Travelling (d) — train is often the most relaxing option for long routes."

Options:
ক. (a) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
খ. (b) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
গ. (c) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন determinerটি উপযুক্ত?
ঘ. (d) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন prepositionটি উপযুক্ত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "an"
- কারণ: "umbrella" শব্দের শুরুতে স্বরবর্ণ-ধ্বনি আছে, তাই অনান্য ইংরেজি নিয়ম অনুযায়ী "an umbrella" হবে।

খ উত্তর: "an"
- কারণ: "unnecessary" শব্দটি স্বরবর্ণ-ধ্বনির সঙ্গে শুরু হওয়ায় "an unnecessary luggage"—তবে সাধারণ কথায় আমরা বলি "unnecessary luggage" (zero article) ও হতে পারে; কিন্তু প্রশ্নের কাঠামোতে যদি একটি article বসাতে হয়, সেক্ষেত্রে "an unnecessary" সঠিক হবে।

গ উত্তর: "a few"
- কারণ: "few"-এর আগে যখন সংখ্যা বা পরিমাণ বোঝাতে ব্যবহার করি এবং গুণগত দিক দিয়ে অনুকূল অর্থে বলতে চাই (কয়েকটা প্রয়োজনীয় জিনিস), তখন "a few" ব্যবহার করা হয়; "few" (without 'a') হলে নেতিবাচক অর্থ ফেলে।

ঘ উত্তর: "by"
- কারণ: পরিবহনে কোন মাধ্যম ব্যবহার করা হচ্ছে তা প্রকাশ করতে ইংরেজিতে "by train", "by bus" ইত্যাদি ব্যবহার করা হয়; সুতরাং "Travelling by train" সঠিক।

Explanation:
এই advisory-তে article ও determiners-বিষয়ক সাধারণ নিয়ম প্রযোজ্য: স্বরবর্ণ-ধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হলে 'an', নির্দিষ্ট পারিবহন মাধ্যমের আগে 'by', পরিমাপ/সংখ্যা বোঝাতে 'a few' ইত্যাদি। (খ)-এর ক্ষেত্রে কথ্যভাবে article না-ও দেওয়া যেতে পারে, তবে প্রশ্নের ফ্রেম অনুযায়ী 'an' যুক্ত করলে উপরের ব্যাখ্যা প্রযোজ্য।

Question #76 (ID: 507203)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A short health tip reads: "To stay healthy, try to have (a) — balanced diet. Avoid (b) — excessive intake of sugar and processed food. Exercise (c) — a regular basis to keep muscles strong. Also try to sleep (d) — adequate hours each night."

Options:
ক. (a) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
খ. (b) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন articleটি উপযুক্ত?
গ. (c) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন preposition/article কম্বিনেশনটি উপযুক্ত?
ঘ. (d) ফাঁক পূরণ করুন — কোন prepositionটি উপযুক্ত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "a"
- কারণ: "balanced diet" এখানে এক ধরণের সাধারণ, countable-conceptual diet বোঝাচ্ছে; "a balanced diet" হল স্বাভাবিক এবং প্রচলিত ব্যবহার।

খ উত্তর: "an"
- কারণ: "excessive" শব্দটি স্বরবর্ণ-ধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু করে, ফলে "an excessive intake" শব্দগুচ্ছটি সঠিক; বাক্যটিতে "avoid an excessive intake of sugar" বলা যায়।

গ উত্তর: "on a"
- কারণ: ইংরেজিতে অভিজ্ঞতা-ভিত্তিক ধারাবাহিকতা প্রকাশ করতে "on a regular basis" ব্যবহার করা হয় ("in a regular basis" ভুল)। তাই "Exercise on a regular basis" সঠিক।

ঘ উত্তর: "for"
- কারণ: ঘুমের সময়কাল বা পরিমাণ নির্দেশ করার ক্ষেত্রে সাধারণত বলা হয় "sleep for adequate hours" বা "sleep for eight hours"; এখানে "for" উপযুক্ত প্রিপোজিশন।

Explanation:
উপরের প্রতিটি ফাঁকের জন্য article এবং preposition-সংক্রান্ত সাধারণ ইংরেজি নিয়ম প্রয়োগ করা হয়েছে: (ক) অনির্দিষ্ট article 'a' ব্যবহৃত—পাঠ্যভিত্তিক, (খ) 'excessive' শব্দটির আগে 'an' লাগে কারণ এটি স্বরবর্ণ-শব্দ দিয়ে শুরু করে, (গ) "on a regular basis" হচ্ছে স্ট্যান্ডার্ড অভিধানিক ফ্রেজ, (ঘ) সময়ে 'for' ব্যবহারে ঘুমের ঘণ্টা প্রকাশ করা হয়।

Question #77 (ID: 507192)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
At this moment Bangladesh confronts (ক) — large number of (খ) — problems related to public health and sanitation. Of all these problems (গ) — sanitation problem is (ঘ) — most pressing issue that needs immediate attention.

Options:
ক. ক: উপযুক্ত শব্দটি বসান (a/an/the/—)?
খ. খ: উপযুক্ত বিশেষণ বা শব্দটি বসান?
গ. গ: উপযুক্ত নিবন্ধ (article) বসান (a/an/the/—)?
ঘ. ঘ: উপযুক্ত বাক্যাংশ বসান (most/very/the most/etc.)?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: a

খ উত্তর: serious

গ উত্তর: the

ঘ উত্তর: the most pressing

Explanation:
ক — 'a large number of' একটি স্থাপিত শব্দগুচ্ছ; এখানে 'a' ব্যবহৃত হয় কারণ 'large number' একক পরিমাপের আগে অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল প্রয়োজন।

খ — 'serious' বিশেষণের মাধ্যমে সমস্যাগুলোকে বর্ণনা করা হচ্ছে; অর্থাৎ 'serious problems' প্রাকৃতিকভাবে ব্যবহারযোগ্য ও অর্থবহ।

গ — যেহেতু আমরা নির্দিষ্ট একটি সমস্যা ('sanitation problem') সম্পর্কে কথা বলছি যা আগের অংশে উল্লিখিত, তাই 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয়।

ঘ — সর্বনামক পর্যায়ে 'most pressing' হল সর্বোচ্চ শ্রেণির তুলনামূলক শব্দ; সুপারলেটিভ ব্যবহারে সাধারণত 'the most ...' লাগে, তাই 'the most pressing' সঠিক।

Question #78 (ID: 507193)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Education remains (ক) — key to national progress in Bangladesh. However (খ) — literacy gap between urban and rural areas remains (গ) — worrying. Addressing (ঘ) — gap will require coordinated policies across sectors.

Options:
ক. ক: উপযুক্ত নিবন্ধ বসান (a/an/the/—)?
খ. খ: কোন শব্দটি সঠিক (a/the/this/—)?
গ. গ: কোন আর্টিকেল বা শব্দ লাগবে (a/an/the/very/etc.)?
ঘ. ঘ: কোন নির্দেশক সর্বনাম লাগবে (this/that/the/—)?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: a

খ উত্তর: the

গ উত্তর: a

ঘ উত্তর: this

Explanation:
ক — 'a key' হল সংগতিপূর্ণ কারণ 'key' এখানে একটি সাধারণ ভূমিকা নির্দেশ করে; 'Education remains a key to...' প্রচলিত ব্যবহার।

খ — 'the literacy gap' নির্দিষ্ট পটভূমিতে (urban vs rural) উল্লেখিত ব্যবধান বোঝানোর জন্য নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল 'the' প্রয়োজন।

গ — 'remains a worrying' তে 'a' প্রয়োজন কারণ 'worrying' একটি বিশেষণযুক্ত বস্তুকে নির্দেশ করছে ('a worrying gap')।

ঘ — পূর্বে উল্লেখিত বিরাট ব্যবধানকে পুনরায় নির্দেশ করতে 'this gap' ব্যবহার উপযুক্ত; এটি পাঠকের সামনে আসা নির্দিষ্ট বিষয়টি সঠিকভাবে নির্দেশ করে।

Question #79 (ID: 507194)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Rural employment in Bangladesh offers (ক) — mixture of opportunities and challenges for households. In many districts (খ) — agricultural sector remains (গ) — primary source of income, while (ঘ) — informal sector provides seasonal and supplemental work.

Options:
ক. ক: কোন আর্টিকেল ব্যবহার করবেন (a/an/the/—)?
খ. খ: আর্টিকেল প্রয়োজন কি (a/the/—)?
গ. গ: কোন শব্দটি উপযুক্ত (a/the/main/—)?
ঘ. ঘ: কোন নির্দেশক বা আর্টিকেল লাগবে (the/this/—)?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: a

খ উত্তর: the

গ উত্তর: the

ঘ উত্তর: the informal sector

Explanation:
ক — 'a mixture' ব্যবহার করা হয় কারণ এখানে সাধারণভাবে বিভিন্ন ধরনের সুযোগ-চ্যালেঞ্জের জটিল মিশ্রণ বোঝানো হচ্ছে; অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল 'a' সঠিক।

খ — যখন নির্দিষ্ট ভূ-অঞ্চল (many districts) প্রসঙ্গে 'agricultural sector' বলা হচ্ছে এবং সেটি প্রসঙ্গে নির্দিষ্টভাবে ব্যবহৃত হচ্ছে, তখন 'the' ব্যবহার উপযুক্ত: 'In many districts the agricultural sector...'.

গ — 'the primary source' ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে কারণ এটি প্রধান উৎস হিসেবে নির্দিষ্টকরণ করছে; সুতরাং 'the' দরকার।

ঘ — এখানে আমরা নির্দিষ্ট খাত ('informal sector') সম্পর্কে বলছি যা বাক্যের পূর্বাংশের ধারাবাহিক অংশ; সাধারণত 'the informal sector' ব্যবহার করে সেটি উপস্থাপন করা হয়।
