Question #80 (ID: 507171)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the passages below by filling each blank with the correct article or determiner (a, an, the, some, any, no, many, much, few, little) so the sentences read naturally.

Options:
ক. (a) _____ elephant is (b) _____ large mammal. (c) _____ African elephant is (d) _____ largest land animal. In (e) _____ wild they travel in herds and eat (f) _____ variety of plants.
খ. (a) There was (b) _____ honest student in the class who always did (c) _____ best. (d) _____ teacher praised him for (e) _____ effort.
গ. (a) _____ apple a day keeps (b) _____ doctor away, they say. (c) _____ fruit contains (d) _____ vitamins and (e) _____ fiber.
ঘ. (a) She bought (b) _____ umbrella because (c) _____ sky looked cloudy. (d) She also carried (e) _____ small towel.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) An (b) a (c) The (d) the (e) the (f) a
খ (a) an (b) an (c) her (d) The (e) her
গ (a) An (b) the (c) The (d) many / some (e) some / a little (either appropriate depending on emphasis)
ঘ (a) an (b) an (c) the (d) a (e) a small / some

Explanation:
ক: (a) 'An' before vowel sound 'elephant'. (b) 'a' before consonant 'large' describing one member of class. (c,d) 'The' because we refer to a specific known species (African elephant) and then the unique title 'the largest'. (e) 'the wild' refers to a known environment (in the wild). (f) 'a variety' uses the indefinite article with 'variety' meaning 'a range of'.

খ: (a) 'an' before vowel sound 'honest' (silent h). (b) 'an' again before vowel. (c) 'her' is appropriate because we refer to the student's own best effort; 'the best' could also be used if intended generally. (d) 'The teacher' — definite because a specific teacher is meant. (e) 'her effort' — matches the student referenced.

গ: (a) 'An' before vowel sound 'apple'. (b) 'the doctor' is a fixed idiom: "keeps the doctor away." (c) 'The fruit' can be 'Fruit' in general — both 'Fruit contains' (zero article) or 'The fruit contains' if referring to fruit in the proverb. (d) 'many' or 'some' vitamins (countable/uncountable choice): 'many vitamins' is common. (e) 'some fiber' or 'a little fiber' (fiber is uncountable), both acceptable depending on emphasis.

ঘ: (a) 'an' before vowel sound 'umbrella' (note: 'an umbrella' — some speakers use 'a' if pronounced with a consonant-like glide, but standard is 'an'). (b) 'an' before 'umbrella' repeated? Here (b) is redundant; interpreted as 'an umbrella' if sentence structure repeated. (c) 'the sky' — definite because it's the sky above. (d) 'a' small towel (one of many). (e) 'a small' or 'some' towel — 'a small towel' is natural. 

Notes: Several blanks admit more than one correct determiner depending on nuance (e.g., 'some' vs 'many', 'the fruit' vs 'fruit' in general). I gave the most natural, commonly accepted choices and explained alternatives where applicable.

Question #81 (ID: 507172)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Fill the blanks in these short narratives with suitable articles, demonstratives, or quantifiers so the meaning becomes precise and natural.

Options:
ক. (a) I saw (b) _____ unusual bird in (c) _____ garden yesterday. (d) _____ bird had (e) _____ bright red feathers.
খ. (a) He needs (b) _____ hour to finish (c) _____ report. (d) He will take (e) _____ short break.
গ. (a) There isn't (b) _____ milk left in (c) _____ fridge. (d) Could you buy (e) _____ liters at (f) _____ market?
ঘ. (a) (b) _____ book on (c) _____ table belongs to (d) _____ student sitting by the window. (e) _____ book is full of notes.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) an (b) an (c) the (d) The (e) some / striking bright red feathers
খ (a) an (b) an (c) the (d) a (e) a short
গ (a) any / no (b) any (c) the (d) some / a couple of (e) the
ঘ (a) The / That (b) The / That (c) the (d) the (e) The / That

Explanation:
ক: (a,b) 'an unusual bird' — 'unusual' begins with a vowel sound; repeat 'an' if structure needs it. (c) 'the garden' — a particular garden (context: one already known or visible). (d) 'The bird' definite because it's the one just mentioned. (e) 'some bright red feathers' — 'some' quantifies uncountable or plural attribute; 'striking' is an optional adjective.

খ: (a,b) 'He needs an hour...' — 'hour' begins with vowel sound. (c) 'the report' — specific report being discussed. (d) 'a short break' — indefinite single break; (e) 'a short' is shorthand but 'a short break' more natural.

গ: (a) When asking about absence, 'There isn't any milk left' or 'There is no milk left'—both correct. (b) 'any' fits negative/question contexts for uncountable nouns. (c) 'the fridge' — the specific fridge you share. (d) 'some liters' or 'a couple of liters' — number needed; 'some' is natural. (e) 'the market' — a known market in context.

ঘ: Use definite demonstratives because we point to a specific book: (a,b) 'That book on the table belongs to the student...' or 'The book on the table belongs...' (c) 'the table' — specific. (d) 'the student' — the one specified by position. (e) 'The book is full of notes' — definite reference. 

Notes: Several blanks can accept more than one correct determiner depending on the context and emphasis (e.g., 'some' vs 'a couple of', 'any' vs 'no'). I have chosen the most idiomatic choices and indicated alternatives.

Question #82 (ID: 507173)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Complete the short informational snippets using appropriate articles, quantifiers, or demonstratives so that the facts read correctly.

Options:
ক. (a) _____ Internet has changed (b) _____ way we access information. (c) In (d) _____ early days, (e) _____ connection was (f) _____ dial-up link.
খ. (a) _____ research shows that (b) _____ regular exercise reduces (c) _____ risk of many diseases. (d) Even (e) _____ small amount each day helps.
গ. (a) She adopted (b) _____ cat from (c) _____ shelter. (d) (e) _____ animal was (f) very timid at first.
ঘ. (a) In (b) _____ experiment, scientists used (c) _____ sample of (d) _____ cells and observed (e) _____ change after (f) several hours.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) The (b) the (c) the (d) the (e) the (f) a / an (a dial-up link — use 'a')
খ (a) Research / The research (b) regular (c) the / a (d) Even (e) a / a small
গ (a) a (b) a (c) the (d) The (e) The (f) very
ঘ (a) the (b) the (c) a (d) the (e) a (f) several

Explanation:
ক: (a,b) 'The Internet' and 'the way' are definite; we refer to a specific global system and the general method. (c,d,e) 'In the early days' and 'the connection was the dial-up link' — 'the' for historically specific period and type of connection. (f) 'a dial-up link' — introducing one instance or type ('a' is fine).

খ: (a) 'Research shows' can be used without article when speaking generally; 'The research' is also acceptable if referencing a particular study. (b) 'regular exercise' — no article for general concept. (c) 'the risk' or 'a risk' — 'the risk of many diseases' is common idiomatically. (d,e) 'Even a small amount each day helps' — 'a' quantifies a singular small measurable amount.

গ: (a) 'She adopted a cat' — indefinite because new. (b) 'a cat from the shelter' — 'the shelter' if specific local shelter, otherwise 'a shelter' if unspecified. (d,e) 'The animal was very timid' — now definite because we've introduced it; 'The animal' refers back to that cat. (f) 'very timid' — adverb not requiring article.

ঘ: (a,b) 'In the experiment' or 'In an experiment' depending on specificity. If the sentence refers to a particular study just mentioned, use 'the experiment'; if introducing, use 'an experiment'. (c) 'a sample' — one sample of many possible. (d) 'the cells' — specific cells used. (e) 'a change' — one observed alteration. (f) 'several hours' — plural quantifier, no article.

Notes: Articles and determiners depend on whether the noun is being introduced for the first time (use 'a/an') or referred to again or uniquely (use 'the'). Quantifiers like 'some', 'several', 'many', and demonstratives like 'this/that' can substitute depending on emphasis; I've given the most natural, commonly used choices and clarified alternatives.

Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags:

Question:
Rapid urbanization has strained city services, created informal settlements, and increased pressure on infrastructure and health systems. Complete the following short passages about urban challenges by filling each blank with an appropriate word or short phrase.

Options:
ক. The city has seen an (a) ______ influx of migrants from rural areas. As a result, housing demand (b) ______ while affordable units remain (c) ______. Many families are forced to live in (d) ______ conditions.
খ. Traffic congestion has (a) ______ scheduled travel times; vehicular emissions (b) ______ air quality, and noise pollution (c) ______ public health.
গ. Urban water supply is often (a) ______, causing households to rely on (b) ______ sources that may be (c) ______.
ঘ. To tackle slum growth authorities must implement (a) ______ urban planning and provide (b) ______ access to basic services such as (c) ______ and (d) ______.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক The city has seen an unprecedented influx of migrants from rural areas. As a result, housing demand has surged while affordable units remain scarce. Many families are forced to live in substandard conditions.

খ Traffic congestion has lengthened scheduled travel times; vehicular emissions degrade air quality, and noise pollution affects public health.

গ Urban water supply is often unreliable, causing households to rely on alternative sources that may be contaminated.

ঘ To tackle slum growth authorities must implement comprehensive urban planning and provide reliable access to basic services such as clean water and sanitation.

Explanation:
ক: (a) 'unprecedented' emphasizes a very large, unusual influx of migrants. (b) 'has surged' indicates a sharp increase in demand. (c) 'scarce' means affordable units are in short supply. (d) 'substandard' describes poor-quality housing typical in informal settlements.

খ: (a) 'lengthened' describes how congestion increases travel time. (b) 'degrade' is used for worsening air quality. (c) 'affects' signals a negative impact on public health.

গ: (a) 'unreliable' captures intermittent or insufficient municipal water supply. (b) 'alternative' refers to non-municipal sources (wells, tanker water). (c) 'contaminated' warns these alternatives can be unsafe.

ঘ: (a) 'comprehensive' signals broad, coordinated planning rather than piecemeal measures. (b) 'reliable' access stresses consistency. (c)-(d) 'clean water' and 'sanitation' are core basic services necessary for healthy living and slum upgrading. Each chosen word fits the context and conveys the typical policy and practical concerns in rapidly urbanizing settings.

ঘ Effective responses include stricter enforcement of environmental laws, widespread adoption of cleaner technology, and active community participation in monitoring.

গ: (a) 'heavy' specifies the type of toxic metals that persist and accumulate. (b) 'unsafe' alerts that contaminated produce is not fit for consumption.

ঘ: (a) 'stricter' highlights the need for stronger regulatory action. (b) 'widespread' encourages broad uptake of low-emission technologies. (c) 'active' emphasizes that community involvement (reporting, local monitoring) strengthens accountability and early detection. Each term was chosen for clarity and to reflect common policy and environmental-health language.

Question #85 (ID: 507182)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Growing populations, changing diets, and climate stress increase food demand and vulnerability. Complete the following statements to reflect typical causes and responses related to food security and agricultural resilience.

Options:
ক. Rising population means per capita food demand (a) ______, while arable land per person (b) ______. This narrows the margin for food security.
খ. Climate variability causes (a) ______ yields; extreme events like droughts and floods (b) ______ crop losses and (c) ______ income for farmers.
গ. To improve resilience, farmers can adopt (a) ______ practices such as crop rotation, (b) ______ irrigation, and (c) ______ seed varieties.
ঘ. Policies to ensure food security should focus on (a) ______ infrastructure, (b) ______ market access, and (c) ______ targeted social safety nets.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক Rising population means per capita food demand increases, while arable land per person decreases. This narrows the margin for food security.

খ Climate variability causes lower yields; extreme events like droughts and floods cause crop losses and reduce income for farmers.

গ To improve resilience, farmers can adopt sustainable practices such as crop rotation, drip irrigation, and drought‑tolerant seed varieties.

ঘ Policies to ensure food security should focus on rural infrastructure, improved market access, and effective targeted social safety nets.

Explanation:
ক: (a) 'increases' captures rising demand as population and consumption grow. (b) 'decreases' reflects the declining share of arable land per person as population grows or land is lost.

খ: (a) 'lower' indicates reduced average yields caused by variable weather. (b) 'cause' links extreme events to direct physical losses of crops. (c) 'reduce' shows the economic consequence for farm incomes.

গ: (a) 'sustainable' practices improve long-term productivity and soil health. (b) 'drip' irrigation is a water‑efficient method often recommended to boost resilience. (c) 'drought‑tolerant' seed varieties are practical adaptations to more frequent dry spells.

ঘ: (a) 'rural infrastructure' (roads, storage, irrigation) reduces post‑harvest loss and connects farmers to markets. (b) 'improved market access' allows producers to sell surplus and obtain inputs. (c) 'effective targeted social safety nets' protect the most vulnerable during shocks and help stabilize demand. Each choice aligns with standard policy recommendations for strengthening food security and resilience.

গ (e) a; (f) x

Question #89 (ID: 507108)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
———– 21st February has become (a) ———– day of remembrance for Bangladesh. On this day we honour (b) ———– martyrs of the language movement who sacrificed (c) ———– lives for the right to speak our mother tongue. The event strengthened (d) ———– cultural identity and inspired (e) ———– generations to come. Every year people gather (f) ———– Shaheed Minar and observe the day with (g) ———– solemn silence. We remember (h) ———– brave souls and pay (i) ———– tribute to their sacrifice, keeping (j) ———– memory alive.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(f).
গ. Fill blanks (g)–(h).
ঘ. Fill blanks (i)–(j).


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) On — 'On 21st February' is the standard prepositional phrase to indicate the day an event occurs.  (b) the — we refer to a specific group of martyrs, so the definite article 'the' is used.  (c) their — 'sacrificed their lives' is the natural possessive pronoun here.

খ (d) the — 'the cultural identity' points to a specific identity formed by the movement.  (e) future — 'inspired future generations' fits standard usage; alternatively 'generations to come' pairs with 'future'.  (f) at — 'gather at Shaheed Minar' is the correct preposition for meeting at a location.

গ (g) with — 'observe the day with solemn silence' uses 'with' to indicate manner.  (h) the — 'the brave souls' refers to the specific martyrs remembered on the day.

ঘ (i) our — 'pay our tribute' shows collective national respect.  (j) their — 'keeping their memory alive' correctly uses the possessive pronoun referring back to the martyrs.

Explanation:
Detailed reasoning: (a) 'On' is used to indicate a specific date. (b) and (d) use the definite article 'the' because we refer to a particular, known group (the martyrs / the cultural identity). (c) and (j) use 'their' to link the action to the martyrs. (e) 'future' pairs naturally with 'generations to come' and conveys continuing influence. (f) 'at' is the correct preposition for meeting at a physical monument (Shaheed Minar). (g) 'with' indicates the manner in which people observe the day, and (i) 'our' expresses collective national respect. The choices prioritize natural collocations and correct grammar for date phrases, articles, possessives, and prepositions.

Question #90 (ID: 507109)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
———– 26th March 1971 is remembered as (a) ———– historic day when the declaration of independence changed (b) ———– destiny of Bangalees. The people endured (c) ———– prolonged struggle and paid (d) ———– heavy price in human lives. That proclamation rallied (e) ———– people across the country and set (f) ———– course towards freedom. Ceremonies are held (g) ———– towns and villages, and families honour (h) ———– lost relatives. We show (i) ———– gratitude to the heroes and renew (j) ———– pledge to build a prosperous nation.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(f).
গ. Fill blanks (g)–(h).
ঘ. Fill blanks (i)–(j).


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) On — standard preposition for dates. (b) the — 'the destiny' because it refers to a specific, shared destiny of the people. (c) a — 'a prolonged struggle' is the common idiom to describe a lengthy conflict.

খ (d) a — 'paid a heavy price' is the fixed expression used to indicate severe losses. (e) the — 'the people' refers to the population of the country (definite). (f) a — 'set a course' is the idiom meaning to begin a path or direction.

গ (g) across — 'across towns and villages' correctly expresses nationwide occurrence. (h) their — 'honour their lost relatives' uses the possessive to refer back to the families' own members.

ঘ (i) our — 'show our gratitude' indicates collective national feeling. (j) our — 'renew our pledge' again uses the collective possessive to indicate a shared promise.

Explanation:
Notes on choices: (a) 'On' is used for specific calendar dates. (b) and (e) use 'the' because they denote particular, known entities (the destiny, the people). (c) and (d) use the indefinite article 'a' as part of common collocations ('a prolonged struggle', 'a heavy price'). (f) 'set a course' is an idiomatic phrase meaning to begin a direction or effort. (g) 'across' emphasizes distribution throughout the country; (h) uses 'their' to refer to the families’ own lost relatives. (i) and (j) are 'our' to show collective responsibility and emotion.

Question #91 (ID: 507110)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
———– 16th December is celebrated as (a) ———– day of victory when the nation regained (b) ———– sovereignty. On that occasion the bravery of (c) ———– fighters is remembered, and we honour (d) ———– sacrifices. The triumph placed Bangladesh (e) ———– an independent position among nations and strengthened (f) ———– sense of national pride. Streets are decorated (g) ———– flags; schools and offices organize (h) ———– programs. Citizens offer flowers at memorials and observe (i) ———– moment of silence to recall (j) ———– fallen heroes.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(f).
গ. Fill blanks (g)–(h).
ঘ. Fill blanks (i)–(j).


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a — 'a day of victory' is the natural noun phrase. (b) its — 'the nation regained its sovereignty' uses the possessive pronoun referring to Bangladesh. (c) the — 'the fighters' refers to the specific freedom fighters of 1971.

খ (d) their — 'honour their sacrifices' uses the possessive relating sacrifices to the fighters. (e) in — 'placed Bangladesh in an independent position' uses 'in' for location/metaphorically among nations. (f) the — 'the sense of national pride' refers to a specific feeling shared by the nation.

গ (g) with — 'decorated with flags' is the correct preposition. (h) cultural — 'organize cultural programs' matches common practice on national days; 'programs' is plural and 'cultural' describes them.

ঘ (i) a — 'observe a moment of silence' is the fixed expression. (j) the — 'recall the fallen heroes' uses the definite article because specific heroes are meant.

Explanation:
Rationale: (a) uses the indefinite article 'a' because 'day of victory' is a descriptive noun phrase. (b) 'its' denotes possession (sovereignty belonging to the nation). (c) and (d) use 'the' and 'their' to refer to specific fighters and their sacrifices. (e) 'in' is used to indicate placement 'in an independent position among nations' (other acceptable phrasing is 'among', but 'in' with 'position' is natural). (f) 'the sense' points to the particular, collective emotion. (g) 'with' is the correct preposition for ornamentation; (h) 'cultural programs' reflects common events held on such days. (i) 'a moment of silence' is a fixed collocation; (j) 'the fallen heroes' uses 'the' to indicate known, particular individuals being commemorated.

Question #92 (ID: 507096)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Rabindranath Tagore was (a) — towering Bengali polymath who was born in (b) — Jorasanko mansion on (c) — banks of (d) — Hooghly river. He became (e) — first non-European to win (f) — Nobel Prize in Literature. From (g) — young age he was exposed to (h) — rich cultural life of his family. He wrote (i) — Gitanjali and many other works that shaped (j) — modern Bengali literature.

Options:
ক. পূর্ণ করুন: (a), (b), (c)
খ. পূর্ণ করুন: (d), (e)
গ. পূর্ণ করুন: (f), (g)
ঘ. পূর্ণ করুন: (h), (i), (j)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a — (b) the — (c) the.  
বিস্তারিত: 'a towering Bengali polymath'—একজন অজ্ঞাতসাধারণ ব্যক্তি হিসাবে 'a' ব্যবহৃত। 'the Jorasanko mansion'—নামসহ নির্দিষ্ট ভবন হলে 'the' প্রয়োজন। 'the banks'—নদীর তীরে অবস্থিত অংশটি নির্দিষ্ট হওয়ায় 'the'।

খ (d) the — (e) the.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the Hooghly river'—নদীর নামের আগে সাধারণত 'the' লাগে। 'the first non-European'—ধর্ম, জাত বা শ্রেণি নির্দিষ্ট করে প্রথম হওয়ার ক্ষেত্রে 'the first' ব্যবহার করি।

গ (f) the — (g) a.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the Nobel Prize'—বিশেষ পুরস্কার, নির্দিষ্ট নাম হওয়ায় 'the'। 'a young age'—সাধারণভাবে 'from a young age' বলে, অ-নির্দিষ্ট বয়স শুরু নির্দেশ করতে 'a' লাগে।

ঘ (h) the — (i) x — (j) x.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the rich cultural life'—পরিবারের নির্দিষ্ট সাংস্কৃতিক জীবনকে বোঝাচ্ছে, তাই 'the'। 'Gitanjali'—গ্রন্থের নাম সাধারণত নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল ছাড়াই ব্যবহৃত (no article)। 'modern Bengali literature'—সাধারণ ধারণা, নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল ছাড়া ব্যবহার করা হয় (no article)।

Explanation:
সংক্ষেপে আর্টিকেল নির্বাচন করার নিয়মগুলি: 'a/an' ব্যবহার করা হয় একক, অ-নির্দিষ্ট কাউকে/কিছু বোঝাতে; 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয় নির্দিষ্ট ব্যক্তি/স্থান/বস্তুকে বোঝাতে বা যখন প্রসঙ্গ থেকে নির্দিষ্টত্ব বোঝা যায়; কখনও কখনও নাম (ব্যক্তি, গ্রন্থ) বা বিমূর্ত সাধারণ ধারণার আগে আর্টিকেল থাকে না (x)। এখানে—'a towering...' যখন Tagore-কে একটি অ-নির্দিষ্ট শ্রেণিতে পরিচয় করানো হচ্ছে; ভবন এবং নদীর নামের ক্ষেত্রে নির্দিষ্ট হওয়ায় 'the' প্রয়োগ; 'first' এবং 'Nobel Prize' যেমন নির্দিষ্ট হওয়ায় 'the' লাগে; 'from a young age' কৌতুকভাবে সাধারণ অভিজ্ঞতা শুরু নির্দেশ করে, তাই 'a'। 'Gitanjali' এবং 'modern Bengali literature' সাধারণ নাম/ধারণা হিসেবে আর্টিকেল ছাড়া ভালো পড়ে।

Question #93 (ID: 507097)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Kazi Nazrul Islam was (a) — revolutionary poet and musician who was born in (b) — Churulia in (c) — Burdwan district. His poetry often spoke against (d) — injustice and for (e) — human dignity. At one point he served as (f) — soldier in (g) — British Indian Army before becoming (h) — prominent voice of Bengali resistance.

Options:
ক. পূর্ণ করুন: (a), (b)
খ. পূর্ণ করুন: (c), (d)
গ. পূর্ণ করুন: (e), (f)
ঘ. পূর্ণ করুন: (g), (h)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a — (b) x.  
বিস্তারিত: 'a revolutionary poet'—কোনো নির্দিষ্ট ব্যক্তি নয়, তাই 'a'। 'in Churulia'—নামবিশিষ্ট গ্রামের ক্ষেত্রে সাধারণত আর্টিকেল ছাড়া 'in Churulia' লেখা হয় (no article)।

খ (c) the — (d) x.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the Burdwan district'—জেলা বা প্রশাসনিক একককে পরিভাষাগতভাবে নির্দিষ্ট করা হলে 'the' অনুচিত নয় (এখানে 'the Burdwan district' প্রাকটিক্যাল)। 'against injustice'—অবিচারের সাধারণ ধারণা, আর্টিকেল ছাড়া ব্যবহার হয়।

গ (e) x — (f) a.  
বিস্তারিত: 'for human dignity'—মানব মর্যাদাকে সাধারণ ধারণা হিসেবেই বলা হয়েছে, তাই আর্টিকেল লাগে না। 'as a soldier'—পেশা/পদবীর ক্ষেত্রে অ-নির্দিষ্ট একক বোঝাতে 'a' ব্যবহৃত হয়।

ঘ (g) the — (h) a.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the British Indian Army'—একটি নির্দিষ্ট সামরিক সংস্থা, তাই 'the'। 'a prominent voice'—কোনো নির্দিষ্ট ব্যক্তিকে নয়, একটি গোষ্ঠীর মধ্যে একজন হিসেবে 'a' ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।

Explanation:
আলাদা নির্দেশনা: রাষ্ট্রীয়/সংগঠনিক নামের আগে প্রায়শই 'the' লাগে (the United Nations, the British Indian Army)। ভুমিকাসূচক পেশা বা পরিচয়ে 'a/an' ব্যবহার করা হয় (a soldier, an artist)। সাধারণ ধারণা বা বিমূর্ত নাম (injustice, human dignity)–এ আর্টিকেল সাধারণত থাকে না। ভৌগলিক গ্রাম/শহরের নামের আগে আর্টিকেল না থাকা স্বাভাবিক (in Churulia), কিন্তু প্রশাসনিক ইউনিট (the Burdwan district)–এ 'the' ব্যবহার করা যায় কারণ এটি নির্দিষ্ট এলাকাকে নির্দেশ করে।

Question #94 (ID: 507099)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Ahsan Manzil was (a) — magnificent pink palace located on (b) — banks of (c) — Buriganga river in (d) — Dhaka. It was once (e) — residence of (f) — Nawabs of Dhaka and is now (g) — museum visited by (h) — tourists from (i) — many countries.

Options:
ক. পূর্ণ করুন: (a), (b)
খ. পূর্ণ করুন: (c), (d)
গ. পূর্ণ করুন: (e), (f), (g)
ঘ. পূর্ণ করুন: (h), (i)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a — (b) the.  
বিস্তারিত: 'a magnificent pink palace'—একটি অ-নির্দিষ্ট বাদামি/এক ধরনের প্রাসাদ হিসেবে 'a'। 'on the banks'—নদীর তীরকে বোঝাতে সাধারণত 'the banks' বলা হয়।

খ (c) the — (d) x.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the Buriganga river'—নদীর নামের আগে স্বাভাবিকভাবে 'the'। 'in Dhaka'—শহরের নামের আগে আর্টিকেল লাগে না (no article)।

গ (e) the — (f) the — (g) a.  
বিস্তারিত: 'the residence'—এই ভবনটি নির্দিষ্টভাবে বাসস্থান হিসেবেই উল্লেখ হলে 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয়। 'the Nawabs of Dhaka'—নোয়াবগণের একটি নির্দিষ্ট গোষ্ঠী/উপাধি, তাই 'the' প্রযোজ্য। 'is now a museum'—একটি ধরণের স্থানে রূপান্তরিত হওয়ায় 'a museum' বলা হয়, কারণ এটি ছিল/হয় একটি ধরণের প্রতিষ্ঠান।

ঘ (h) x — (i) x.  
বিস্তারিত: 'tourists'—সাধারণভাবে বহিঃপ্রবাহের দর্শনার্থীদের বোঝাতে আর্টিকেল ছাড়া 'tourists' ব্যবহার করা যায়। 'many countries'—পরিমাণসূচক বহুবচনবিশিষ্ট শব্দের আগে আর্টিকেল লাগে না ('from many countries')।

Explanation:
নিয়মের সারমর্ম: আবাস/প্রতিষ্ঠান/প্রাসাদের পরিচয়ে 'a' বা 'the' নির্ভর করে নির্দিষ্টতা ও পরিচিতির উপর। নদী বা তীরের ক্ষেত্রে 'the' বহুল প্রচলিত ('the Ganges', 'the Buriganga', 'on the banks')। শহর/গ্রামের নামের আগে সাধারণত আর্টিকেল থাকে না ('in Dhaka', 'in London')। গোষ্ঠী/পদ বা ঐতিহ্যবাহী শিরোনামের ক্ষেত্রে (the Nawabs) 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয়। 'tourists from many countries'—উভয়ই সাধারণ প্রকাশ, আর্টিকেল ছাড়াই সঠিক।

Question #95 (ID: 507102)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Over (a) — past decade, (b) — metropolitan region has experienced worsening air quality, according to (c) — National Air Monitoring Agency. (d) — smog often blankets the city during winter months. Many people now suffer from (e) — chronic respiratory illnesses, and hospitals report (f) — increase in asthma-related admissions. Experts warn that unless (g) — problem is tackled, (h) — public health will continue to decline.

Options:
ক. প্যাসেজের (a) ও (b) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
খ. প্যাসেজের (c) ও (d) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
গ. প্যাসেজের (e) ও (f) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
ঘ. প্যাসেজের (g) ও (h) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the, (b) the
খ (c) the, (d) The
গ (e) × (no article), (f) an
ঘ (g) the, (h) × (no article)

Explanation:
(a) the — 'the past decade' is a definite period known to speaker and listener; use the definite article.
(b) the — 'the metropolitan region' refers to a specific, previously identified urban area.
(c) the — named government or national agencies normally take 'the' because they are unique institutions (the National Air Monitoring Agency).
(d) The — sentence-initial reference to a particular phenomenon (smog that affects the city) takes the definite article; capitalization in the passage can be retained as 'The'.
(e) × (no article) — 'chronic respiratory illnesses' is a plural noun used generically; plural count nouns commonly appear without an article when speaking generally.
(f) an — 'an increase' requires the indefinite article 'an' because 'increase' begins with a vowel sound and refers to a singular, countable event.
(g) the — 'the problem' points back to the specific air-quality problem already described; definite article required.
(h) × (no article) — 'public health' is an uncountable abstract noun used in a general sense and typically appears without an article.

Question #96 (ID: 507103)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In (a) — last century, wildlife managers celebrated when (b) — endemic tortoise species was removed from (c) — brink of extinction on (d) — remote island. Nonetheless, (e) — invasive rodents later posed a new threat. The ministry launched (f) — comprehensive eradication program and, as a result, (g) — population of ground-nesting birds began to recover. Now (h) — prospects for long-term ecological restoration look brighter.

Options:
ক. প্যাসেজের (a) ও (b) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
খ. প্যাসেজের (c) ও (d) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
গ. প্যাসেজের (e) ও (f) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
ঘ. প্যাসেজের (g) ও (h) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the, (b) the
খ (c) the, (d) a
গ (e) × (no article), (f) a
ঘ (g) the, (h) the

Explanation:
(a) the — 'the last century' refers to a specific, commonly-referenced time span; use the definite article.
(b) the — when referring to a particular species already identified by context, 'the endemic tortoise species' is definite.
(c) the — 'the brink of extinction' is a fixed phrase denoting a specific critical state; use 'the'.
(d) a — 'a remote island' indicates one among possibly several remote islands; indefinite article 'a' is correct because the island is not uniquely specified earlier.
(e) × (no article) — 'invasive rodents' is a plural noun used generally to describe the category of animals posing threat; no article needed for plural generic reference.
(f) a — 'a comprehensive eradication program' uses the indefinite article because it introduces one such program.
(g) the — 'the population of ground-nesting birds' refers back to the specific local population affected earlier; definite article is appropriate.
(h) the — 'the prospects' or 'the prospects for long-term ecological restoration' points to a particular evaluative outlook being discussed; 'the' makes it definite.

Question #97 (ID: 507104)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
By (a) — mid-century, analysts warn that (b) — millions of people living in low-lying zones could be displaced by sea-level rise. In (c) — absence of coordinated international responses, (d) — such displacement would further burden (e) — already strained economies. (f) Greater international cooperation and (g) — sustainable coastal planning are essential to avoid (h) — humanitarian crisis.

Options:
ক. প্যাসেজের (a) ও (b) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
খ. প্যাসেজের (c) ও (d) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
গ. প্যাসেজের (e) ও (f) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।
ঘ. প্যাসেজের (g) ও (h) ফাঁকগুলোতে উপযুক্ত article বসান।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the, (b) × (no article)
খ (c) the, (d) such
গ (e) already strained economies — × (no article) or optionally 'the' depending on context; best: ×
ঘ (g) × (no article), (h) a

Explanation:
(a) the — 'the mid-century' is a specific temporal reference (mid-21st century); use 'the'.
(b) × (no article) — 'millions of people' is an indefinite, large number used generically; we do not use 'the' here unless referring to a specific, previously identified group.
(c) the — the fixed phrase 'in the absence of' requires the definite article.
(d) such — 'such displacement' is idiomatic here: 'such' refers back to the displacement just described; 'the displacement' could also work, but 'such' emphasizes the kind/scale of displacement.
(e) × (no article) — 'already strained economies' is a plural, general reference to economies that are strained; no article is acceptable for general plural reference. If the writer means those specific economies already mentioned, 'the already strained economies' could be used; in this context the generic form without article is natural.
(f) Greater — this word begins the phrase and does not need an article: 'Greater international cooperation...'.
(g) × (no article) — 'sustainable coastal planning' is an uncountable/abstract activity used generically; no article required.
(h) a — 'a humanitarian crisis' is one instance of a crisis; the indefinite article 'a' is appropriate because it introduces the type of crisis that might occur.

Question #98 (ID: 507081)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Diogenes was famous for carrying (a) ____ lamp even in (b) ____ daytime, saying he was searching for (c) ____ honest man. One afternoon (d) ____ child began to tease him and called him (e) ____ eccentric. Diogenes put (f) ____ lamp under his arm and walked to (g) ____ market. The onlookers found (h) ____ whole scene surprisingly amusing.

Options:
ক. Fill in blanks (a) এবং (b)
খ. Fill in blanks (c) এবং (d)
গ. Fill in blanks (e) এবং (f)
ঘ. Fill in blanks (g) এবং (h)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a lamp; (b) broad (→ "in broad daytime" commonly phrased as "in broad daylight", so here "broad" completes the idiom). 
খ (c) an honest man; (d) a child. 
গ (e) an eccentric; (f) his lamp. 
ঘ (g) the market; (h) the whole scene.

Explanation:
Answers and reasoning:
- (a) 'a lamp' — use the indefinite article 'a' because we introduce one lamp (consonant sound 'l').
- (b) 'broad' — the common fixed expression is 'in broad daylight'. The passage gives 'daytime', so 'broad' completes the idiom; alternatively the phrase could be written 'in the daytime' but 'in broad daylight' is idiomatic.
- (c) 'an honest man' — 'honest' begins with a vowel sound (silent 'h'), so use 'an'.
- (d) 'a child' — introducing a non-specific single child uses 'a'.
- (e) 'an eccentric' — 'eccentric' begins with a vowel sound, so 'an' is correct.
- (f) 'his lamp' — 'his' shows possession (he carried it), so 'his lamp' is most natural.
- (g) 'the market' — a specific market that people make reference to in the town; use 'the'.
- (h) 'the whole scene' — 'whole scene' is definite and specific, so 'the' is appropriate.
General notes: choose 'a/an' for non-specific singular nouns (based on vowel/consonant sounds), 'the' for specific or previously-mentioned nouns, and use possessives (his/her) when ownership is implied. Idiomatic phrases (e.g., 'in broad daylight') should be preserved.

Question #99 (ID: 507082)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Confucius often spent mornings listening while others spoke. In (a) ____ nearby village lived (b) ____ old musician who played (c) ____ wooden flute at dawn. One day (d) ____ musician came with (e) ____ question and asked Confucius (f) ____ advice about composing a new tune. Confucius offered (g) ____ brief reply and the musician left with (h) ____ contented look.

Options:
ক. Fill in blanks (a) এবং (b)
খ. Fill in blanks (c) এবং (d)
গ. Fill in blanks (e) এবং (f)
ঘ. Fill in blanks (g) এবং (h)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a nearby village; (b) an old musician. 
খ (c) a wooden flute; (d) the musician. 
গ (e) a question; (f) for some advice (→ "asked for some advice"). 
ঘ (g) a brief reply; (h) a contented look.

Explanation:
Why these choices work:
- (a) 'a nearby village' — the village is introduced as one among possibly many, so use the indefinite article 'a'.
- (b) 'an old musician' — 'old' begins with a vowel sound, so 'an' is used for a non-specific single person.
- (c) 'a wooden flute' — 'a' introduces a single, unspecified instrument; 'wooden' describes the flute.
- (d) 'the musician' — after mentioning 'an old musician', referring back to him uses the definite article 'the' because he is now specific in the context.
- (e) 'a question' — an unspecified single query brought to Confucius.
- (f) 'for some advice' — the verb 'ask' commonly takes 'for' when requesting help: 'asked for advice'; 'some' softens the noun and is natural here.
- (g) 'a brief reply' — indefinite article for a non-specific short answer.
- (h) 'a contented look' — 'a' introduces the look as one instance of an expression.
Grammar tips: use 'a/an' to introduce non-specific singular nouns, switch to 'the' when that noun becomes specific or previously mentioned, and include prepositions like 'for' when required by the verb (e.g., 'ask for advice').

Question #100 (ID: 507083)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A stoic poet lived by (a) ____ sea and taught (b) ____ young apprentice to notice (c) ____ small changes in tides and (d) ____ vastness of the sky. One dusk (e) ____ apprentice grew impatient and demanded (f) ____ quick secret to fame. The poet brewed (g) ____ tea, smiled, and told him that (h) ____ truth often arrives slowly.

Options:
ক. Fill in blanks (a) এবং (b)
খ. Fill in blanks (c) এবং (d)
গ. Fill in blanks (e) এবং (f)
ঘ. Fill in blanks (g) এবং (h)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the sea; (b) his young apprentice. 
খ (c) the small changes; (d) the vastness of the sky. 
গ (e) the apprentice; (f) a quick secret (or 'a quick trick'). 
ঘ (g) some tea; (h) the truth.

Explanation:
Detailed reasoning:
- (a) 'the sea' — when speaking of the sea in relation to where someone lives, 'the sea' is idiomatic (specific body of water relative to that home).
- (b) 'his young apprentice' — 'his' indicates the poet's pupil; use the possessive rather than an indefinite article to show the relationship.
- (c) 'the small changes' — these are the particular changes the poet pointed out, so make them definite.
- (d) 'the vastness of the sky' — 'the vastness' is a specific quality being referred to; 'of the sky' makes it definite.
- (e) 'the apprentice' — refers back to the previously-mentioned apprentice, so use 'the'.
- (f) 'a quick secret' (or 'a quick trick') — an indefinite single thing demanded; either word is acceptable depending on nuance ('secret' emphasizes knowledge, 'trick' emphasizes a shortcut).
- (g) 'some tea' — natural in English when offering an uncountable beverage in a non-specific amount.
- (h) 'the truth' — 'truth' here is definite, the particular truth the poet refers to; we can say 'the truth often arrives slowly'.
Article guidance: use 'the' for specific, known, or previously-mentioned items; use 'a/an' for introducing non-specific singular nouns; use possessives to show relationships; use 'some' for unspecified amounts of uncountable nouns.

Question #101 (ID: 507078)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Dhaka city is undergoing (a) _____ influx of people from (b) _____ rural areas. This rapid growth has strained (c) _____ infrastructure and created (d) _____ housing crisis.

Options:
ক. (a) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসাবেন? 
খ. (b) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসাবেন? 
গ. (c) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসাবেন? 
ঘ. (d) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসাবেন? 


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an — কারণ "influx" শব্দটি স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হওয়ায় পূর্বে অ-বিবেচক আর্টিকেল হিসেবে "an" ব্যবহার করা উপযুক্ত।
খ the — এখানে "the rural areas" ব্যবহার করে ধরে নেয়া হয়েছে যে ঢাকায় আসা মানুষগুলো নির্দিষ্ট গ্রামীণ এলাকার থেকে আসছে; তাই নির্দিষ্টতা দেখাতে "the" উপযুক্ত।
গ the — "infrastructure" সাধারণত অসংখ্য উপাদানের সমষ্টি এবং নির্দিষ্ট পরিস্থিতিতে নির্দিষ্ট অবকাঠামোকে নির্দেশ করলে "the infrastructure" ব্যবহার করা হয়।
ঘ a — "housing crisis" একটি গণ্য করা সমস্যার নাম, তাই অনির্দিষ্ট সংকট বোঝাতে "a" ব্যবহৃত হয়েছে।

Explanation:
বিস্তারিত ব্যাখ্যা:
ক: "influx" শব্দটি [iŋ-flʌks] — স্বরধ্বনি (i-) দিয়ে শুরু হয়; English grammar অনুযায়ী স্বরধ্বনী শব্দের আগে "an" আর্টিকেল ব্যবহার করা হয় (উদাহরণ: an apple, an hour)। এখানে "an influx" বলতে একটি উল্লেখযোগ্য প্রবাহ বোঝানো হয়েছে, তাই "an" সঠিক।
খ: "from the rural areas" বা "from rural areas" — উভয়ই ব্যবহারযোগ্য, তবে বাক্যটিতে ঢাকায় আসা মানুষের উৎস হিসেবে নির্দিষ্ট গ্রামীণ অঞ্চলগুলোকে ইঙ্গিত করা হলে "the rural areas" সঠিকভাবে নির্দিষ্টতা দেয়। তাই "the" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।
গ: "infrastructure" শব্দটি সাধারণত অবকাঠামোর সমষ্টি বোঝায়; যখন কোন শহরের সামগ্রিক অবকাঠামোকে চিহ্নিত করা হয় (পানিসহ ব্যবস্থা, সড়ক, নিকাশী ইত্যাদি) তখন "the infrastructure" বলা যায়। এখানে ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে নির্দিষ্ট অবকাঠামোর উপর চাপের কথা বোঝাতে, সুতরাং "the" প্রয়োজন।
ঘ: "a housing crisis" — এখানে একটি অনির্দিষ্ট তবে বাস্তব সংকটকে নির্দেশ করা হয়েছে; ইংরেজিতে এমন ক্ষেত্রে অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল "a" ব্যবহৃত হয়।
সংক্ষেপে: বাক্যের স্বরূপ এবং নির্দিষ্টতা বিবেচনা করে উপরের আর্টিকেল/বিশেষণগুলো উপযুক্ত।

Question #102 (ID: 507079)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Although Bangladesh has (a) _____ literacy rate compared to past decades, the quality of education in many districts remains (b) _____. Teachers often lack (c) _____ training and classrooms have (d) _____ basic facilities.

Options:
ক. (a) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বা শব্দগুচ্ছ বসাবেন?
খ. (b) স্থানে কোন বিশেষণ বসাবেন?
গ. (c) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসালে উপযুক্ত হবে?
ঘ. (d) স্থানে কোন শব্দ বসাবেন?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a higher — "literacy rate" তুলনা করা হচ্ছে অতীত দশকের সঙ্গে, তাই তুলনামূলক বিশেষণ ব্যবহার করা প্রয়োজন: "a higher literacy rate"।
খ inadequate — শিক্ষা মানের অবনতি বোঝাতে "inadequate" (অপর্যাপ্ত/অপ্রতুল) উপযুক্ত।
গ proper — শিক্ষকরা প্রয়োজনীয় দক্ষতা ও প্রশিক্ষণ থেকে বঞ্চিত, তাই "proper training" অর্থে "proper" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।
ঘ very few — ক্লাসরুমগুলোতে গুরুত্বপূর্ণ সুবিধাগুলি অপ্রতুল; "very few basic facilities" বলে এ অবস্থা শ্রুতিবদ্ধভাবে বোঝানো হয়েছে।

Explanation:
বিস্তারিত ব্যাখ্যা:
ক: বাক্যটি তুলনামূলক (compared to past decades), তাই আমরা এমন একটি বিশেষণ চাই যা তুলনা প্রকাশ করে: "higher", "improved" ইত্যাদি। সাধারণ ইংরেজিতে সম্পূর্ণ করে বললে "a higher literacy rate" সঠিক। এখানে "a" লাগে কারণ "literacy rate" একটি গণ্যনীয় পরিমাপ।
খ: "the quality of education... remains _____" — এখানে মানকে নেগেটিভভাবে তুলনা করা হচ্ছে; "inadequate" মানে পর্যাপ্ত না, যা অর্থপূর্ণভাবে প্রয়োগযোগ্য। অন্য বিকল্প যেমন "variable" বা "uneven" হলেও প্রশ্নের প্রসঙ্গে "inadequate" বেশি স্পষ্ট।
গ: "Teachers often lack (c) _____ training" — সাধারণভাবে বলা হয় "lack proper training"; "proper" এখানে যোগ্যতা ও প্রয়োজনীয়তা বোঝায়। "adequate training" ও চলতে পারে কিন্তু বাক্যটিতে সাধারণ রূপে "proper" বেশি প্রাকটিক্যাল।
ঘ: "classrooms have (d) _____ basic facilities" — এটি একটি পরিমাণগত অভাব নির্দেশ করে; "very few basic facilities" অর্থাৎ খুব কম মৌলিক সুবিধা আছে, যা মূলনীতিগত সমস্যা নির্দেশ করে।
ভাষাগতভাবে এসব শব্দ বিকল্প হিসেবে বদলানো যেতে পারে, তবে উপরের পছন্দগুলো বাক্যের অর্থ ও স্বর বজায় রেখে ঠিকঠাক ফিট করে।

Question #103 (ID: 507080)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The coastal villages are facing (a) _____ threat from (b) _____ rising sea levels. Many families have to move because (c) _____ salinity pollutes their (d) _____ drinking water.

Options:
ক. (a) স্থানে কোন বিশেষণ বসাবেন?
খ. (b) স্থানে কোন আর্টিকেল বা শব্দ বসাবেন?
গ. (c) স্থানে কোন শব্দ ব্যবহার করবেন?
ঘ. (d) স্থানে কোন বিশেষণ বা শব্দ বসাবেন?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a growing — "a growing threat" বলতে ক্রমান্বয়ে বাড়তে থাকা বিপদের কথা বোঝে; তাই "a growing" উপযুক্ত।
খ the — "the rising sea levels" বলতে নির্দিষ্ট এক ঝুকি/ঘটনা বোঝানো হচ্ছে (বিশ্বস্ত তথ্য অনুযায়ী সাগরের উচ্চতা বাড়ছে), তাই "the" ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে।
গ excessive — সমুদ্রের লবণ পদার্থের মাত্রা বেড়ে যাওয়াকে বোঝাতে "excessive salinity" ঠিক বলে; অর্থাৎ অত্যধিক স্যালিনিটি।
ঘ potable — "potable drinking water" বলতে পানের উপযোগী পানি বুঝায়; এখানে স্যালিনিটি সেই পানিকে অযোগ্য করে তুলছে বলে "potable" সঠিক শব্দ।

Explanation:
বিস্তারিত ব্যাখ্যা:
ক: "threat" শব্দের আগে একটি নির্ণায়ক বিশেষণ লাগবে যা তার মাত্রা বা প্রকৃতি বলে; "a growing threat" বলে ধীরে ধীরে বাড়তে থাকা সমস্যাকে বোঝায় — উপকূলীয় গ্রামগুলোর জন্য উপযুক্ত বর্ণনা।
খ: "rising sea levels" সাধারণ একটি বিশ্বব্যাপী ঘটনা, কিন্তু বাক্যে তা নির্দিষ্টভাবে ওই এলাকার জন্য প্রাসঙ্গিক হওয়ায় "the rising sea levels" বলা যায় — এইভাবে নির্দিষ্ট ঘটনা/পরিবর্তনকে নির্দেশ করা হয়।
গ: "salinity pollutes their drinking water" — এখানে স্যালিনিটি’র মাত্রা বাড়ার কারণেই পানীয় জল দূষিত হচ্ছে; তাই "excessive" বা "increased" ব্যবহার করা যায়; "excessive" বেশি স্পষ্টভাবে অতি মাত্রাটিকে বলেন।
ঘ: "drinking water"-এর গুণগত দিক বোঝাতে ব্যবহার করা হয়েছে "potable" (পানীয় যোগ্য)। বাক্যটি বলছে স্যালিনিটির কারণে তাদের potable water কমে বা দূষিত হচ্ছে; তাই "potable" শব্দটি উপযুক্ত।
সামগ্রিকভাবে এই শব্দচয়ন পরিবেশগত কারণে সৃষ্ট বাস্তব সমস্যার থিমের সঙ্গে সামঞ্জস্যপূর্ণ।

Question #110 (ID: 507033)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Late one (a) ——— evening, an old baker noticed (b) ——— loaf missing from (c) ——— counter. He peered around and even looked under (d) ——— bright wooden table, but the loaf was nowhere to be seen.

Options:
ক. Fill in blank (a) with the correct article/determiner.
খ. Fill in blank (b) with the correct article/determiner.
গ. Fill in blank (c) with the correct article/determiner.
ঘ. Fill in blank (d) with the correct article/determiner.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a
খ a
গ the
ঘ the

Explanation:
ক (a = a): We use 'a' with 'evening' in the phrase 'Late one a evening' (more naturally: 'Late one evening' or 'a late evening'); here 'a' signals one unspecified instance of evening. খ (b = a): 'a loaf' is indefinite — the baker notices one loaf missing (not a previously specified loaf), so 'a' is appropriate. গ (c = the): 'the counter' is definite because it refers to the specific counter in the baker's shop. ঘ (d = the): 'the bright wooden table' is definite as it points to a particular table in the scene. Overall, use 'a' for introducing something non-specific and 'the' when the noun is specific or known in context.

Question #116 (ID: 507021)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Monsoon arrived early this year and with it a sharp rise in mosquito‑borne illnesses. The local clinic reports many fever cases and parents worry about their youngsters. The municipal notice reads: (a) — _____ rise in dengue cases has been observed. For (b) — _____ children and the elderly these infections are particularly risky. Small puddles, buckets and clogged drains are (c) — _____ for mosquito breeding. Therefore the notice urges (d) — _____ community participation to eliminate these sites.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a): choose the correct article/phrase to complete the sentence.
খ. Fill blank (b): supply the correct words to refer to vulnerable groups.
গ. Fill blank (c): supply the appropriate adjective describing water that allows mosquito reproduction.
ঘ. Fill blank (d): give the best noun phrase to indicate the required collective response.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "a"
খ উত্তর: "children and the elderly"
গ উত্তর: "standing" (or "stagnant")
ঘ উত্তর: "collective community action" (or "community participation")

Explanation:
ক: The sentence "(a) — _____ rise in dengue cases has been observed" needs an indefinite article because we are reporting one instance of an observed rise: "a rise in dengue cases." Using "the" would imply a specific previously known rise; "a" is the natural choice.

খ: Vulnerable groups should be referred to as "children and the elderly." English commonly uses the definite article with "elderly" ("the elderly"); combining both gives the clear phrase "children and the elderly." This correctly identifies the groups at higher risk.

গ: Mosquitoes breed in "standing" or "stagnant" water — water that does not flow and remains in containers, puddles or drains. Both adjectives are acceptable; "standing" is very common in public‑health messaging.

ঘ: The notice calls for community‑level effort. Phrases like "collective community action" or simply "community participation" convey that residents must work together (cleaning, removing breeding sites, reporting stagnant water) to reduce mosquito populations.

Question #117 (ID: 507022)

Question:
The neighbourhood park has become a favourite spot for families, but lately many visitors complain about constant mosquito buzzing at dusk. A volunteer leaflet reads: To reduce the problem we must (a) — _____ all potential breeding sites, report (b) — _____ drains, and use (c) — _____ measures such as bed nets and repellents. Remember: prevention is better than cure; organise (d) — _____ drives every month.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a): choose the verb phrase meaning to remove places where mosquitoes breed.
খ. Fill blank (b): complete the phrase referring to malfunctioning drains.
গ. Fill blank (c): name the adjective describing immediate personal protection steps.
ঘ. Fill blank (d): suggest the correct noun to describe coordinated community activities.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "eliminate" or "remove"
খ উত্তর: "blocked or clogged drains"
গ উত্তর: "protective" (as in "protective measures")
ঘ উত্তর: "clean‑up drives" or "vector control drives"

Explanation:
ক: "Eliminate" or "remove" potential breeding sites is the correct public‑health instruction: dispose of containers, clean gutters, and eliminate standing water.

খ: Drains that do not flow properly are often described as "blocked" or "clogged drains." Reporting these to municipal services helps prevent stagnant pools.

গ: "Protective measures" is the natural phrase for actions individuals take to avoid bites (bed nets, repellents, coils, appropriate clothing).

ঘ: Community efforts are commonly called "clean‑up drives" or "vector control drives." Regular monthly drives help remove debris and standing water, reducing mosquito breeding over time.

Question #118 (ID: 507023)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A school health poster warns pupils about mosquitoes and offers tips: Sleep under (a) — _____ when camping or sleeping outdoors. Apply an EPA‑approved (b) — _____ to exposed skin before dusk. Eliminate (c) — _____ such as flower‑pot saucers and discarded tyres from your compound. Note that some species bite mostly during (d) — _____ hours, so be extra careful then.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a): name the best physical barrier used while sleeping outdoors.
খ. Fill blank (b): give the general name of a topical substance preventing bites.
গ. Fill blank (c): identify the collective noun for small water‑holding objects that breed mosquitoes.
ঘ. Fill blank (d): specify the time of day when certain mosquitoes (Aedes) are most active.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "insecticide‑treated bed net" (or "ITN")
খ উত্তর: "insect repellent" (e.g., DEET or picaridin)
গ উত্তর: "containers" or "water‑holding containers" (e.g., saucers, tyres)
ঘ উত্তর: "daytime" (especially early morning and late afternoon)

Explanation:
ক: An insecticide‑treated bed net (ITN) provides both a physical barrier and chemical protection while sleeping outdoors; it is recommended for malaria prevention.

খ: Topical insect repellents (DEET, picaridin, IR3535) applied to exposed skin before going outdoors reduce bites. The poster should advise an EPA‑approved repellent.

গ: Mosquitoes like Aedes species lay eggs in small "containers" or "water‑holding containers" — any object that can hold a little water (flower‑pot saucers, discarded tyres, cans). Removing or emptying these prevents breeding.

ঘ: Aedes mosquitoes (which transmit dengue, chikungunya and Zika) are primarily daytime biters, with peak activity in early morning and late afternoon. This contrasts with Anopheles mosquitoes (malaria) that bite mostly at night.

ঘ more

Explanation:
ক — 'much easier' is a common collocation where 'much' intensifies the comparative 'easier.' 'Far' could also work, but 'much' is natural here. 

খ — 'both' correctly introduces a dual-language situation: 'both in English and the local language.' 

গ — 'into' is the proper preposition when translating something from one language into another ('translate notes into a visitor's language'). 

ঘ — 'more' is the comparative used with 'inclusive' to indicate a greater degree of inclusivity ('more inclusive').

খ an

Question #128 (ID: 506988)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
As urban populations swell, securing reliable water supplies for cities and industry becomes a pressing challenge. Planners must balance demand management, infrastructure upgrades and climate risks to ensure communities have safe water for decades to come. The following passage highlights key choices that decision‑makers face.

Options:
ক. Fill (a) in the passage: "meeting (a) ———— rising demand for potable water"
খ. Fill (b) in the passage: "Conservation is (b) ———— immediate strategy"
গ. Fill (c) in the passage: "infrastructure investment requires (c) ———— long‑term planning"
ঘ. Fill (d) in the passage: "rainfall patterns may become (d) ———— unpredictable"


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক the
খ an
গ a
ঘ increasingly

Explanation:
ক — "the": The phrase "meeting the rising demand" uses the definite article because we refer to a specific, known trend (the rising demand). "Meeting a rising demand" would be possible but changes nuance to any unspecified rise.

খ — "an": "an immediate strategy" requires the indefinite article "an" before a vowel sound; it indicates one of the first responses. "Conservation is immediate strategy" would be ungrammatical.

গ — "a": The noun phrase "a long‑term planning" is slightly awkward; the intended structure is "requires a long‑term plan" or "requires long‑term planning." Here the blank is best filled with "a" if the following word is "long‑term plan", or omitted if using "requires long‑term planning." Given the provided prompt, "a long‑term planning" is nonstandard, so the natural fill is "a" assuming "a long‑term plan" is implied.

ঘ — "increasingly": "Become increasingly unpredictable" is the common collocation: "increasingly" modifies the adjective "unpredictable" to show that unpredictability is growing over time. Alternatives like "more" are possible but "increasingly" is stylistically stronger and idiomatic.

Question #129 (ID: 506989)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Decarbonizing transport requires changes in vehicles, fuels and urban design. Policymakers must weigh technological options, grid capacity and social equity to avoid leaving vulnerable communities behind while reducing emissions.

Options:
ক. Fill (a): "Transitioning will require (a) ———— shift in technology and behavior"
খ. Fill (b): "Electric vehicles are (b) ———— part of the solution"
গ. Fill (c): "only if electricity is (c) ———— generated from low‑carbon sources"
ঘ. Fill (d): "Policies must be crafted to avoid (d) ———— unintended social harms"


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a fundamental
খ a key
গ predominantly
ঘ causing

Explanation:
ক — "a fundamental": The phrase "a fundamental shift" is idiomatic to describe deep, structural changes in technology and behavior. "Fundamental" emphasizes the scale of change required.

খ — "a key": "a key part of the solution" is a common collocation indicating something is important but not the only element. "An integral" or "a major" could also work, but "a key" is concise and clear.

গ — "predominantly": The sentence implies that EVs reduce emissions only when the electricity that charges them comes largely from low‑carbon sources. "Predominantly generated" conveys that the majority of generation should be low‑carbon. Alternatives like "primarily" would also fit.

ঘ — "causing": "Avoid causing unintended social harms" uses the gerund "causing" after "avoid" to indicate the action policies should prevent. Other verbs (e.g., "creating") are possible, but "causing" directly links policy choices to adverse outcomes to be avoided.

Question #130 (ID: 506990)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Sustainable agriculture seeks to raise yields while protecting soils, reducing pollution and conserving water. Farmers, researchers and policymakers are exploring mixed approaches — from regenerative practices to precision nutrient management — to meet global food needs without degrading the land.

Options:
ক. Fill (a): "Reducing (a) ———— dependence on synthetic fertilizers is a priority"
খ. Fill (b): "Regenerative methods can be (b) ———— effective at restoring soil organic matter"
গ. Fill (c): "However, some alternatives demand (c) ———— more labor or time"
ঘ. Fill (d): "Precision agriculture aims to apply nutrients (d) ———— where they are needed"


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক excessive
খ highly
গ significantly
ঘ precisely

Explanation:
ক — "excessive": "Excessive dependence" conveys an unhealthy or unsustainable level of reliance on synthetic fertilizers that can lead to pollution and soil decline. "Reducing dependence" without "excessive" is weaker in tone.

খ — "highly": "Highly effective" is the standard collocation to indicate strong positive results. "Very effective" could be used but "highly" is slightly more formal and fits the register.

গ — "significantly": The adverb "significantly" modifies "more labor or time" to indicate a substantial increase in resource requirements, which is often true of some low‑input or organic approaches.

ঘ — "precisely": "Apply nutrients precisely where they are needed" captures the goal of precision agriculture: to target inputs at the right place and time for efficiency and reduced runoff. Words like "only" or "exactly" could work, but "precisely" is idiomatic here.

Question #131 (ID: 506961)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Once you have completed a diagnostic screening of your learners, you must select instructional content that suits their prior knowledge, learning preferences, and the course objectives. Frequently teachers treat content choice and assessment as separate tasks. However, the (A) ——— between assessment procedures and learning materials is crucial to ensure that what is taught is the same as what is measured.

Options:
ক. Blank (A)টিতে কোন শব্দটি পূরণ করবেন?
খ. Blank (B)টিতে উপযুক্ত শব্দটি কী হবে?
গ. Blank (C)টিতে কোন শব্দটি সর্বোত্তম?
ঘ. Blank (D)টিতে কী শব্দটি নিখুঁত?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "comprehensive" 
খ উত্তর: "individual" 
গ উত্তর: "separate" 
ঘ উত্তর: "alignment"

Explanation:
ক: "comprehensive" (বিস্তৃত/পূর্ণাঙ্গ) ব্যবহার করলে বাক্যটি বোঝায় যে পরীক্ষাটি গভীর ও সমগ্রমুখী, যা শিক্ষার্থীর দক্ষতা ও প্রয়োজন নিরূপণের জন্য উপযুক্ত।

খ: "individual" (ব্যক্তিগত) ব্যবহার করে বোঝানো হয়েছে যে বিষয়বস্তু শিক্ষার্থীদের ব্যক্তিগত পটভূমি ও শিখনশৈলীর সঙ্গে খাপ খায়। এটি collective শব্দের পরিবর্তে উপযুক্ত কারণ পরিকল্পনা ব্যক্তিভিত্তিক অভিযোজনের কথা বলছে।

গ: "separate" (অলাদা) এখানে ব্যবহার করে স্পষ্ট করা হয়েছে যে অনেকে বিষয়বিষয়ক নির্বাচন ও মূল্যায়নকে আলাদা কাজ হিসেবে দেখে — যা সমন্বয়ের অভাব নির্দেশ করে।

ঘ: "alignment" (সামঞ্জস্য/সঙ্গতি) ব্যবহার করলে বাক্যটি স্পষ্ট হয়: মূল্যায়ন পদ্ধতি ও বিষয়বস্তুর মধ্যে সঙ্গতি প্রয়োজন, যাতে শেখানোর বিষয়বস্তু ও মূল্যায়নের লক্ষ্য একই থাকে। এই শব্দটি শিক্ষাগত পরিকল্পনা ও মূল্যায়নের টেকসই সংযোগকে নির্দেশ করে।

Question #132 (ID: 506962)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Before designing a sequence of lessons, after conducting brief formative checks you should align objectives with community context, available resources, and students' interests. Many educators mistakenly treat assessment as an (A) ——— rather than a planning cornerstone; therefore, (B) ——— choice and evaluation strategies should be planned together to secure (C) ——— validity and relevance.

Options:
ক. Blank (A)টিতে কোন শব্দটি বসাবেন?
খ. Blank (B)টিতে উপযুক্ত শব্দটি কী হবে?
গ. Blank (C)টিতে কোন পরিভাষাটি সঠিক?
ঘ. Blank (D)টিতে অন্য কোন শব্দ অন্তর্ভুক্ত করলে বাক্যটি বদলে যাবে?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: "afterthought" 
খ উত্তর: "curriculum" 
গ উত্তর: "construct" 
ঘ উত্তর: "alignment"

Explanation:
ক: "afterthought" (পরে মনে পড়া, পরবর্তীতে যুক্ত করা) দিয়ে বোঝানো হচ্ছে শিক্ষকমহলে মূল্যায়নকে প্রায়ই 'বাঁধা দেয়া' কাজে পরিণত করা হয়, অর্থাৎ আগে থেকে পরিকল্পনায় অন্তর্ভুক্ত করা হয় না।

খ: "curriculum" (পাঠ্যসূচী/কোর্সবিষয়) এখানে অর্থবহ কারণ পাঠ্যবস্তু ও শেখানোর কৌশল একসঙ্গে পরিকল্পিত হলে মূল্যায়নও লক্ষ্যবহ হবে।

গ: "construct" (গঠন/ধারণা) একটি টেকনিক্যাল শব্দ; "construct validity" মানে যে মূল্যায়ন যেটা মাপার কথা, সেটাই মাপছে। তাই বাক্যে এটি ব্যবহার করলে প্রাসঙ্গিক বৈজ্ঞানিক অর্থ আসে — পরিকল্পনা ও মূল্যায়ন একসাথে করলে ধারনাগত বৈধতা নিশ্চিত হয়।

ঘ: "alignment" (সঙ্গতি) শব্দটি যুক্ত করলে বাক্যটিতে পাঠ্যবস্তু, মূল্যায়ন ও উদ্দেশ্যের মধ্যে মিলের প্রয়োজনীয়তা জোরদার হবে। উপরের তিনটি উত্তর দিয়ে মিল রেখে বোঝানো হয়েছে যে মূল্যায়ন অনিবার্যভাবে পাঠ্য ও পরিকল্পনার অংশ হওয়া উচিত।

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Early childhood is (a) ———— stage in a person's life. During (b) ———— time parents lay (c) ———— foundation for habits and values. If (d) ———— caregiver provides both love and discipline, the child is likely to develop a balanced personality.

Options:
ক. (a) ———— কী শব্দ দিয়ে পূরণ করবেন?
খ. (b) ———— কী শব্দ দিয়ে পূরণ করবেন?
গ. (c) ———— কী শব্দ দিয়ে পূরণ করবেন?
ঘ. (d) ———— কী শব্দ দিয়ে পূরণ করবেন?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: a
খ উত্তর: this
গ উত্তর: the
ঘ উত্তর: the

Explanation:
ক (a = a): বাক্যটি বলছে 'Early childhood is (a) ———— stage in a person's life.' এখানে অনির্দিষ্ট একটি পর্যায় বোঝাতে 'a stage' সঠিক।

খ (b = this): 'During (b) ———— time parents lay...' এখানে নির্দিষ্টভাবে সেই প্রারম্ভিক সময়ই বোঝানো হচ্ছে, তাই 'this time' অর্থগতভাবে ঠিক।

গ (c = the): 'parents lay (c) ———— foundation'—এখানে বিশেষভাবে কোন ভিত্তি নির্দেশ করা হচ্ছে (মুল্যবোধ ও অভ্যাস গঠনের ভিত্তি), তাই নির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল 'the foundation' ব্যবহার করতে হবে।

ঘ (d = the): 'If (d) ———— caregiver provides...' এখানে নির্দিষ্ট রকমের অভিভাবক বা যত্নদাতা বোঝানো হচ্ছে (যে মানুষটি সন্তানের যত্ন নেয়), তাই 'the caregiver' সঠিক।

After initial readiness tests and community surveys, you select topics that reflect learners' cultural backgrounds, developmental readiness, and future goals. The (A) ——— between topic selection and assessment practices shapes your interpretation of learner outcomes; teachers should avoid viewing evaluation as (B) ——— from instruction and instead treat it as an integral (C) ——— that contributes to (D) ——— student achievement.

ক. Blank (A)টিতে কোন শব্দটি ব্যবহার করবেন?

ঘ উত্তর: "improved"

Explanation:
ক: "alignment" (সঙ্গতি) এখানে উপযুক্ত কারণ এটি নির্দেশ করে যে বিষয়বস্তু ও মূল্যায়ন একে অন্যের সঙ্গে সঙ্গত হলে ফলাফলগুলি অর্থপূর্ণভাবে ব্যাখ্যা করা যায়।

খ: "separate" (অলাদা) ব্যবহার করে বলা হচ্ছে শিক্ষার্থীর মূল্যায়নকে যদি শেখানোর কার্যক্রম থেকে আলাদা ধরা হয়, তখন ফলাফলগুলির ব্যাখ্যা ও ব্যবহার সীমিত হয়।

গ: "component" (অংশ/উপাদান) উল্লেখ করে যে মূল্যায়ন একক উপাদান নয় বরং শিক্ষা প্রক্রিয়ার অভিন্ন অংশ — পাঠ্য, কৌশল, এবং মূল্যায়ন একসঙ্গে কাজ করে।

ঘ: "improved" (উন্নত/সुधারিত) যুক্ত করলে বাক্যটি বোঝায় যে সমন্বিত পরিকল্পনা ও মূল্যায়ন শিক্ষার্থীর অর্জনে উন্নতি নিয়ে আসে। অন্য সমার্থক শব্দও ব্যবহৃত হতে পারে (উদাহরণ: "better" বা "enhanced"), কিন্তু "improved" স্পষ্টভাবে ফলাফলগত উন্নতির দিকটি তুলে ধরে।

Question #135 (ID: 506965)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
An encouraging teacher can transform (a) ———— attitude of a shy pupil. When (b) ———— teacher notices a little progress, (c) ———— praise can boost the child's confidence. Every student should be given (d) ———— fair opportunity to improve.

Options:
ক. (a) ———— কী শব্দটি লাগবে?
খ. (b) ———— কী শব্দটি লাগবে?
গ. (c) ———— কী শব্দটি লাগবে?
ঘ. (d) ———— কী শব্দটি লাগবে?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: the
খ উত্তর: a
গ উত্তর: such
ঘ উত্তর: a

Explanation:
ক (a = the): 'transform (a) ———— attitude of a shy pupil'—এখানে সেই নির্দিষ্ট অবসান/মনোভাবকে বোঝানো হচ্ছে, তাই 'the attitude' ব্যবহার করা যুক্তিযুক্ত।

খ (b = a): 'When (b) ———— teacher notices...'—এখানে কোনও সাধারণ শিক্ষক বোঝানো হচ্ছে, সেজন্য অনির্দিষ্ট আর্টিকেল 'a teacher' উপযুক্ত।

গ (c = such): ' (c) ———— praise can boost...'—এক্ষেত্রে 'such praise' অর্থাৎ 'এমন ধরনের প্রশংসা' ব্যবহার করলে বাক্যটি স্বাভাবিক পড়ে; 'the praise' দিলে দ্বিতীয়াংশ বিভ্রান্ত হতে পারে।

ঘ (d = a): 'given (d) ———— fair opportunity'—অর্থ হলো 'একটি ন্যায্য সুযোগ', যা সাধারণ ভাষায় 'a fair opportunity' বলে দেওয়া হয়।

Question #136 (ID: 506966)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A child's character develops in (a) ———— home environment and (b) ———— community around him. Parents often worry (c) ———— child's future and therefore try to prepare (d) ———— child carefully.

Options:
ক. (a) ———— কী বসবে?
খ. (b) ———— কী বসবে?
গ. (c) ———— কী বসবে?
ঘ. (d) ———— কী বসবে?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: the
খ উত্তর: the
গ উত্তর: about the
ঘ উত্তর: the

Explanation:
ক (a = the): 'develops in (a) ———— home environment'—এখানে সাধারণভাবে কিন্তু নির্দিষ্ট প্রেক্ষাপটে 'the home environment' ব্যবহার করা হয় কারণ কথকটি ঐ নির্দিষ্ট পরিবেশকে বোঝাচ্ছে।

খ (b = the): 'and (b) ———— community around him'—এখানেও একই যুক্তি; ঐ নির্দিষ্ট বা পরিবেশগত সম্প্রদায়কে বোঝাতে 'the community' সঠিক।

গ (c = about the): 'Parents often worry (c) ———— child's future'—ইংরেজিতে 'worry about the child's future' বলে, তাই 'about the' সম্পূর্ণ ফ্রেজ প্রয়োজন।

ঘ (d = the): 'prepare (d) ———— child carefully'—এখানে ঐ নির্দিষ্ট শিশুকে (their child বা the child) প্রস্তুত করার কথা বলা হচ্ছে; সাধারণভাবে 'the child' উপযুক্ত।

Question #137 (ID: 506928)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
As cities expand and electric vehicle adoption accelerates, energy planners face a complex challenge: meeting higher peak loads while accommodating intermittent generation. Smart grids, demand-response programs and storage technologies can help smooth (a) _____ swings in supply and demand. Yet deploying these solutions at scale will require (b) _____ political will and long-term financing. In the short term, fossil fuels may still play (c) _____ role in ensuring reliability, but their environmental costs make that option (d) _____ undesirable.

Options:
ক. ভরাট (a)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
খ. ভরাট (b)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
গ. ভরাট (c)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
ঘ. ভরাট (d)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: the
খ উত্তর: significant
গ উত্তর: a
ঘ উত্তর: increasingly

Explanation:
ক (a = the): ইংরেজিতে নির্দিষ্ট দারুণ বা পরিচিত swings বোঝাতে 'the' ব্যবহার করা হয় — here we refer to the particular supply-and-demand swings just mentioned. খ (b = significant): 'political will and long-term financing' এর পরিমাণ বা গুরুত্ব বোঝাতে 'significant'—'substantial' বা 'considerable'-ও হতে পারে; 'significant' context-appropriate এবং স্বল্প-দৈর্ঘ্যের অনুষঙ্গটি মেনে চলে। গ (c = a): 'play a role' শব্দসমষ্টি ইংরেজিতে প্রচলিত; indefinite article 'a' প্রয়োজন। ঘ (d = increasingly): বাক্যটি তুলনামূলকভাবে সময়ের সাথে খারাপ হওয়া বোঝাচ্ছে — 'increasingly undesirable' মানে ক্রমেই কম পছন্দনীয়; 'increasingly' একটি adverb যা 'undesirable' শ্রেণির adjective modify করে। বিকল্পভাবে 'ever more' বা 'progressively' ব্যবহার করা যেত, কিন্তু 'increasingly' সবচেয়ে স্বাভাবিক।

Question #138 (ID: 506929)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Remote communities are often cut off from the main grid, making local solutions attractive. Small-scale solar installations coupled with battery storage can create (a) _____ reliable microgrids that reduce dependence on diesel. However, successful deployment depends on (b) _____ maintenance regimes and trained local technicians. For investors, predictable tariffs and (c) _____ regulatory frameworks are essential. If these factors are absent, projects risk becoming (d) _____ underutilized or abandoned.

Options:
ক. ভরাট (a)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
খ. ভরাট (b)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
গ. ভরাট (c)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
ঘ. ভরাট (d)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: highly
খ উত্তর: regular
গ উত্তর: clear
ঘ উত্তর: chronically

Explanation:
ক (a = highly): 'highly reliable microgrids' is a common collocation emphasizing strong reliability; alternatives like 'very' are possible but 'highly' is idiomatic. খ (b = regular): onderhoud/maintenance ের জন্য 'regular maintenance regimes' মানে পর্যায়ক্রমিক ও নিয়মিত রক্ষণাবেক্ষণ; 'adequate' বা 'consistent' হতে পারত, কিন্তু 'regular' এখানে উপযুক্ত। গ (c = clear): 'clear regulatory frameworks'—নিয়ম-কানুন ও নীতিমালা যেন অস্পষ্ট না হয়; 'predictable' ও 'stable' ও ব্যবহার করা যেতে পারে; এখানে 'clear' বিশেষ করে নির্দেশনা ও অনুমোদন প্রক্রিয়ার স্বচ্ছতা বোঝায়। ঘ (d = chronically): 'chronically underutilized or abandoned' নির্দেশ করে যে প্রকল্পগুলি নিয়মিতভাবে কম ব্যবহার বা পরিত্যক্ত হয়, ক্রমাগত বা দীর্ঘমেয়াদি সমস্যা বোঝাতে 'chronically' ব্যবহৃত হয়েছে; 'ultimately' বা 'frequently' বিকল্প হতে পারে কিন্তু 'chronically' অর্থগতভাবে শক্তিশালী এবং প্রাসঙ্গিক।

Question #139 (ID: 506930)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
To achieve deep decarbonization, governments are weighing a mixture of subsidies, regulations and market instruments. A well-calibrated carbon price can act as (a) _____ signal to redirect capital toward clean technologies. But if revenue recycling is mishandled, public acceptance may (b) _____ quickly. Complementary policies — for example, targeted support for innovation and workforce retraining — are (c) _____ to ensure a just transition. Without those measures, the climate agenda risks being (d) _____ politically.

Options:
ক. ভরাট (a)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
খ. ভরাট (b)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
গ. ভরাট (c)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন
ঘ. ভরাট (d)‑এর জন্য উপযুক্ত শব্দটি দিন


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: a
খ উত্তর: erode
গ উত্তর: essential
ঘ উত্তর: vulnerable

Explanation:
ক (a = a): 'act as a signal'—এই অভিব্যক্তিটির সঙ্গে indefinite article 'a' সাধারণ ব্যবহার। 'an' লাগবে না কারণ 'signal' শব্দটি শব্দের শুরুতে consonant sound। খ (b = erode): 'public acceptance may erode quickly'—'erode' মানে আস্থা কমে যাওয়া; বাক্যে temporal fragility বোঝাতে উপযুক্ত। বিকল্প হিসেবে 'wane' ব্যবহার করেছিলেও চলে। গ (c = essential): 'are essential to ensure a just transition'—এই ক্ষেত্রে 'essential' সবচেয়ে শক্তিশালী এবং স্পষ্ট; 'critical' বা 'necessary' ও ব্যবহারযোগ্য। ঘ (d = vulnerable): 'the climate agenda risks being vulnerable politically' বোঝায় যে রাজনীতিতে এটি সহজে আঘাতপ্রাপ্ত বা ক্ষতিগ্রস্ত হতে পারে; 'politically vulnerable' প্রচলিত collocation. বিকল্প 'derailed' বা 'undermined' হতে পারত, কিন্তু 'vulnerable' বাক্যের গঠন রক্ষা করে।

Question #140 (ID: 506916)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A tiny orphan boy found (a) — old, dusty book in (b) — attic of (c) — abandoned house. He thought it was (d) — fortune.

Options:
ক. Blank (a): Which article/determiner fits before "old"?
খ. Blank (b): Which article fits before "attic"?
গ. Blank (c): Which article fits before "abandoned house"?
ঘ. Blank (d): Which article fits before "fortune"?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an
খ the
গ an
ঘ a

Explanation:
ক (an): Use "an" before a word that begins with a vowel sound. "Old" begins with the vowel sound /o:/, so "an old, dusty book" is correct.

খ (the): "The attic of the abandoned house" refers to a specific attic belonging to that particular house. Use the definite article "the" for something identifiable or specific.

গ (an): "Abandoned" begins with a vowel sound (/ə/), and we are introducing a house that is not previously specified, so "an abandoned house" is appropriate.

ঘ (a): "Fortune" here means "a large amount of wealth" (countable in this sense as a single unspecified thing). We introduce it for the first time, so the indefinite article "a" is used: "a fortune."

Question #141 (ID: 506917)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There was (a) — scientist who discovered (b) — new element. His discovery was (c) — beginning of (d) — revolution in chemistry.

Options:
ক. Blank (a): Which article fits before "scientist"?
খ. Blank (b): Which article fits before "new element"?
গ. Blank (c): Which article fits before "beginning"?
ঘ. Blank (d): Which article fits before "revolution in chemistry"?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a
খ a
গ the
ঘ a

Explanation:
ক (a): We are introducing one scientist among many, so the indefinite article "a" is used: "a scientist."

খ (a): "New element" is being mentioned for the first time and begins with a consonant sound (/n/), so "a new element" is correct.

গ (the): When we say "the beginning," we refer to a specific start-point of the following event (the discovery led specifically to that start), so the definite article "the" is appropriate: "the beginning of ..."

ঘ (a): "A revolution in chemistry" means one revolution (a significant change) among possible changes. It's introduced as an indefinite, countable event, so use "a." The full phrase: "the beginning of a revolution in chemistry."
