Question:
On (a) — island, there is (b) — lake surrounded by (c) — tall coconut trees. Fishermen call it (d) — "Mirror of Sky".

Options:
ক. Blank (a): Which article fits before "island"?
খ. Blank (b): Which article fits before "lake"?
গ. Blank (c): Which article fits before "tall coconut trees"?
ঘ. Blank (d): Which article fits before the place-name "Mirror of Sky"?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an
খ a
গ the
ঘ the

Explanation:
ক (an): Use "an" before words starting with a vowel sound. "Island" begins with the vowel sound /aɪ/, so "an island" is correct.

খ (a): We are introducing one lake on that island, not previously specified, so the indefinite article "a" is appropriate: "a lake."

গ (the): "The tall coconut trees" identifies a specific group of trees that are surrounding that lake; since they are definite in this context (the ones around the lake), "the" is used.

ঘ (the): When giving a specific name or nickname to a place ("Mirror of Sky"), we commonly use the definite article: "the 'Mirror of Sky'" — it refers to that particular named lake.

Question #143 (ID: 506886)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A calm evening at home is (a) — perfect opportunity to practise language skills. Sitting by the window, one can pick up (b) — newspaper or (c) — novel and spend an hour reading. Such habit sharpens (d) — vocabulary and improves comprehension.

Options:
ক. Blanks (a) কে পূরণ করো
খ. Blank (b) কে পূরণ করো
গ. Blank (c) কে পূরণ করো
ঘ. Blank (d) কে পূরণ করো


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: (a) the — "a calm evening is the perfect opportunity" because we refer to a specific opportunity within the given context.
খ উত্তর: (b) a — "pick up a newspaper" uses the indefinite article because any one newspaper is meant, not a specific paper already known.
গ উত্তর: (c) a — "pick up a novel" similarly takes the indefinite article since it refers to any novel.
ঘ উত্তর: (d) the — "sharpens the vocabulary" uses the definite article because we speak about vocabulary in general as a known concept related to the person reading.

Explanation:
ক: এখানে নির্দিষ্ট সময়ে (that particular time) যে সুযোগ বলা হচ্ছে, তাই 'the' ব্যবহার করি — 'the perfect opportunity'.
খ ও গ: যখন আমরা সাধারণ কোনো একক জিনিস বোঝাই (যেমন কোনো পত্রিকা বা কোনো উপন্যাস), তখন 'a' (indefinite article) ব্যবহার করা উচিত: 'a newspaper', 'a novel'.
ঘ: 'vocabulary' এখানে সাধারণভাবে একটি পরিচিত ধারণা হিসেবে এসেছে — কোনো শিক্ষার্থীর বা ব্যক্তির 'the vocabulary' উন্নত হয়; বাক্যে নির্দিষ্ট অর্থে 'the' ব্যবহার উপযুক্ত।

Question #144 (ID: 506887)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
On a rainy afternoon, (a) — coach called all players for (b) — quick meeting. He reminded them about (c) — importance of teamwork and advised (d) — captain to prepare a revised plan for practice.

Options:
ক. Blank (a) পূরণ করো
খ. Blank (b) পূরণ করো
গ. Blank (c) পূরণ করো
ঘ. Blank (d) পূরণ করো


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: (a) the — 'the coach' because we refer to a specific coach already understood in context (the team's coach).
খ উত্তর: a — 'a quick meeting' uses the indefinite article as it is one meeting among possible meetings, not previously specified.
গ উত্তর: the — 'the importance of teamwork' uses 'the' because we are talking about a specific, known concept: the importance that was being emphasized.
ঘ উত্তর: the — 'the captain' uses 'the' since within a team there is a particular captain known to all; he is a specific person.

Explanation:
ক: 'coach' কথনটিতে নির্দিষ্ট ব্যক্তিকে নির্দেশ করা হয়েছে (টিমের কোচ), তাই 'the coach' সঠিক।
খ: 'quick meeting' এখানে নতুন একটী সভার কথা বলা হয়েছে, পূর্বপরিচিত নয় — তাই 'a quick meeting'।
গ: 'importance of teamwork' হলো একটি পরিচিত ধারণা বা নির্দিষ্ট বিষয় যা কোচ উল্লেখ করছেন, তাই 'the importance'।
ঘ: 'captain' টিমের নির্দিষ্ট নেতা; সবাই যে ক্যাপ্টেনটিরই কথা বলছে, সেইজনকে বোঝাতে 'the captain' ব্যবহার করা হয়।

Question:
During the beach clean-up drive, (a) — volunteers gathered shells and (b) — plastic bottles. They found (c) — enormous amount of waste near (d) — shoreline which saddened everyone.

Options:

খ. Blank (b) পূরণ করো
গ. Blank (c) পূরণ করো
ঘ. Blank (d) পূরণ করো


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: (a) the — 'the volunteers' because the sentence refers to a particular group taking part in the drive.
খ উত্তর: — (no article) — 'plastic bottles' in plural often takes no article when speaking generally about such items.
গ উত্তর: an — 'an enormous amount of waste' uses 'an' because 'enormous' begins with a vowel sound and we refer to a singular quantity expression 'an amount'.
ঘ উত্তর: the — 'the shoreline' refers to a specific shoreline (the one near the clean-up site), so the definite article is appropriate.

Explanation:
ক: এখানে নির্দিষ্ট কর্মসূচির অংশ হিসেবে যে স্বেচ্ছাসেবীদের কথা বলা হচ্ছে, তারা পরিচিতভাবে 'the volunteers' হয়।
খ: 'plastic bottles' যদি সাধারণভাবে বোঝানো হয় (প্লাস্টিক বোতলগুলো), বিশেষ কোনো নির্দিষ্ট বোতল না বোঝালে কোনো article লাগেনা।
গ: 'enormous amount' শব্দযুগল 'an amount' — 'enormous' স্বরবর্ণ দিয়ে শুরু হওয়ায় 'an' লাগে: 'an enormous amount of waste'.
ঘ: 'shoreline' এখানে সেই নির্দিষ্ট তীররেখার কথা বলা হচ্ছে যেখানেই পরিচ্ছন্নতা অভিযান হচ্ছে, তাই 'the shoreline' যথার্থ।

Options:
ক. (a) শূন্যস্থানটি পূরণ করুন
খ. (b) শূন্যস্থানটি পূরণ করুন
গ. (c) শূন্যস্থানটি পূরণ করুন
ঘ. (d) শূন্যস্থানটি পূরণ করুন


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক উত্তর: 'a' — He fills a notebook every evening because we mean one notebook among many (indefinite article). খ উত্তর: 'the' — He follows the timetable set by his teacher; 'the' specifies that particular timetable already mentioned or known. গ উত্তর: 'an' — He nourishes an ambition; 'ambition' begins with a vowel sound so the indefinite article 'an' is required. ঘ উত্তর: 'an' — He is an example in his class; 'example' begins with a vowel sound, so 'an' is correct.

Also, 'an ambition' means one particular aim or desire (unspecified). ঘ — 'example' starts with a vowel sound (/ɪ/), so 'an example' is grammatically correct. In contexts where we refer to someone who serves as a model for others, 'an example' is idiomatic (e.g., 'an example to his classmates'). Together these choices follow standard English article usage: 'a/an' for indefinite singular nouns and 'the' for definite, specific nouns.

ক (the): 'In the age of information' — we use 'the' because we refer to the specific era defined by information technology.

খ (a): 'a scarce commodity' — 'scarce commodity' is singular and indefinite, so 'a' is appropriate.

গ (their / one's): 'protect their personal data' — 'their' is the natural plural, gender-neutral possessive referring back to 'people'. 'One's' is also grammatically correct but less conversational when referring to people generally.

ঘ (their): 'should not share their passwords' — again 'their' is the inclusive possessive matching 'people'; 'the passwords' would imply a specific set of passwords, which is not intended.

Question #161 (ID: 506835)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Rita was rushing to catch an early train to the city. The short passage below describes what happened. Complete each numbered sub-question by supplying the correct prepositions.

Options:
ক. Rita arrived ___ the station ___ 8 a.m.
খ. She ran ___ the platform and jumped ___ the train.
গ. She kept her bag ___ her lap ___ the journey.
ঘ. She waved ___ her friend ___ the window as the train moved off.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক at; at — Rita arrived at the station at 8 a.m. (use 'arrive at' for places like stations; 'at' for clock times). 
খ across; onto — She ran across the platform and jumped onto the train. ('across' describes moving from one side to the other over the platform; 'onto' indicates movement to a position on the train). 
গ on; during — She kept her bag on her lap during the journey. ('on' shows position resting on the lap; 'during' indicates the time-span of the journey). 
ঘ to; from — She waved to her friend from the window as the train moved off. ('wave to' is the typical collocation; 'from the window' shows the origin of the action).

Explanation:
ক: 'arrive' usually pairs with 'at' for points/places (arrive at the station) and we use 'at' for times like '8 a.m.' — hence 'at the station at 8 a.m.'.

খ: 'run across' fits when moving over the surface of something (the platform). To indicate movement onto the train, use 'onto' (movement toward and ending up on). 'On' would indicate position but not the movement.

গ: A bag rests 'on' a lap. For the time period we use 'during the journey' to indicate throughout that period. 'For the journey' is also possible but 'during' emphasises throughout the journey.

ঘ: We 'wave to' someone (the recipient of the action). 'From the window' shows where she was when she waved. 'At the window' could describe position but 'from the window' better conveys origin of the action while the train is moving.

Question #162 (ID: 506836)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A family went out for a picnic by the riverside. Fill the blanks in each instruction or description using suitable prepositions.

Options:
ক. They set out ___ the morning ___ Sunday.
খ. They spread the mat ___ the grass and sat ___ it.
গ. The children ran ___ the trees ___ the butterflies.
ঘ. They returned ___ sunset, tired but happy ___ memories.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক in; on — They set out in the morning on Sunday. ('in the morning' is the idiomatic phrase; 'on Sunday' for the day).
খ on; on — They spread the mat on the grass and sat on it. ('on' indicates position atop the grass and atop the mat).
গ among; after — The children ran among the trees after the butterflies. ('among the trees' expresses movement within a group of trees; 'after' indicates pursuit).
ঘ at; with — They returned at sunset, tired but happy with memories. ('at sunset' marks that time; 'with memories' shows possession/accompaniment of feelings/memories).

Explanation:
ক: Use 'in the morning' (common English collocation) to indicate part of the day. Days take 'on' (on Sunday).

খ: 'on the grass' indicates being positioned on its surface. Both spreading the mat and sitting are actions that place someone/something on a surface, so 'on' is appropriate twice.

গ: 'among' is used when something or someone moves within a group (trees). To indicate pursuit, 'after' is the suitable preposition (they ran after butterflies).

ঘ: Times like 'sunset' are usually preceded by 'at' (at sunrise, at noon, at sunset). 'With memories' is idiomatic to show that they returned accompanied by memories — i.e., their feelings/memories came with them.

Question #163 (ID: 506837)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Dr. Karim gave post-operative instructions to a patient. Complete the following sentences by inserting the correct prepositions.

Options:
ক. Take the medicine ___ your meals and finish it ___ a week.
খ. Keep the wound covered ___ the daytime but let it breathe ___ night.
গ. Avoid heavy lifting ___ six weeks to allow healing ___ the tissues.
ঘ. If you feel fever ___ 38°C or notice increasing pain, report ___ the clinic immediately.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক after; within — Take the medicine after your meals and finish it within a week. ('after meals' times dosing; 'within a week' gives the allowable time span to complete the course).
খ during; at — Keep the wound covered during the daytime but let it breathe at night. ('during the daytime' for the period; 'at night' is the standard phrase).
গ for; of — Avoid heavy lifting for six weeks to allow healing of the tissues. ('for six weeks' expresses duration; 'healing of the tissues' is the natural prepositional phrase).
ঘ above; to — If you feel fever above 38°C or notice increasing pain, report to the clinic immediately. ('fever above 38°C' indicates the threshold; 'report to' a place/authority is the correct verb–preposition pair).

Explanation:
ক: 'after your meals' tells when to take the medicine relative to eating. 'Within a week' indicates that the course should be completed at some point not later than one week — a time limit.

খ: 'during the daytime' emphasizes the whole daylight period when the wound stays covered; 'at night' is the common time phrase used for nighttime.

গ: 'for six weeks' expresses the length of the restriction. 'Healing of the tissues' uses 'of' to connect the noun 'healing' with what is being healed (the tissues).

ঘ: Medical thresholds for fever are described as 'above' a temperature (or 'over'). 'Report to the clinic' is the standard collocation to indicate informing or visiting the clinic/medical authority.

Question #164 (ID: 506841)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
The playground is (a) — essential area for (b) — school where students (c) — play, run and enjoy. It is (d) — open space surrounded by trees.

Options:
ক. (a) এর স্থানে উপযুক্ত শব্দ লিখুন।
খ. (b) এর স্থানে উপযুক্ত নিবন্ধ/প্রত্যয় লিখুন।
গ. (c) এর স্থানে উপযুক্ত ক্রিয়া বা মডাল লিখুন।
ঘ. (d) এর স্থানে উপযুক্ত নিবন্ধ লিখুন।


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an
খ the
গ can
ঘ an

Explanation:
ক: 'essential' শব্দটি স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হওয়ায় এর আগে অসংজ্ঞায়ক নিবন্ধ 'an' ব্যবহার করা হবে: 'an essential area'.

খ: এখানে নির্দিষ্ট স্কুলকে বোঝানো হচ্ছে (স্কুল = আগে থেকেই প্রসঙ্গিত), তাই নির্দিষ্ট নিবন্ধ 'the' ব্যবহার করা উচিত: 'for the school'.

গ: বাক্যতে 'students ... play, run and enjoy' — ক্রিয়াগুলো করার সক্ষমতা বা অনুমতাকে বোঝাতে 'can' সবচেয়ে উপযুক্ত মডাল: 'students can play'. বিকল্প হিসেবে 'may' বা 'often' ব্যবহার করলে অর্থ পরিবর্তিত হতে পারে, কিন্তু সাধারণ বিবৃতির জন্য 'can' যথাযথ।

ঘ: 'open space' কথাটির আগে অসংজ্ঞায়ক নিবন্ধ 'an' প্রয়োজন কারণ 'open' স্বরধ্বনি দিয়ে শুরু হয়: 'an open space'.

অতএব পূর্ণ বাক্যটি হবে: 'The playground is an essential area for the school where students can play, run and enjoy. It is an open space surrounded by trees.'

Question:
A computer lab is (a) — modern facility in (b) — school. It contains (c) — computers, printers and (d) — projector for teaching.

Options:
ক. (a) এর স্থানে কোন নিবন্ধ বসবে?
খ. (b) এর স্থানে কোন নিবন্ধটি প্রাসঙ্গিক?
গ. (c) এর স্থানে উপযুক্ত পরিমাণসূচক শব্দ দিন।
ঘ. (d) এর স্থানে কোন নিবন্ধ ব্যবহার করবেন?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a
খ the
গ several
ঘ a

Explanation:
ক: 'modern facility' বলতে একটির কথা বলা হচ্ছে, কোন নির্দিষ্ট নয়; তাই অসংজ্ঞায়ক নিবন্ধ 'a' ব্যবহার করা হয়: 'a modern facility'.

খ: এখানে প্রসঙ্গভিত্তিকভাবে ওই প্রতিষ্ঠানের কম্পিউটার ল্যাবকে বোঝানো হচ্ছে — তা নির্দিষ্ট; ফলে 'the school' সঠিক: 'in the school'.

গ: 'computers, printers and a projector'—কম্পিউটারগুলোর সংখ্যাটি অনিশ্চিত কিন্তু একাধিক বোঝাতে 'several' বা 'many' ব্যবহার করা যায়। সাধারণভাবে 'several' প্রাসঙ্গিক ও সংক্ষিপ্ত।

ঘ: 'projector' একটি একক উপকরণ; আগে নির্দিষ্টভাবে উল্লেখ না করলে 'a projector' ব্যবহার করা উচিত: 'a projector for teaching'.

পূর্ণ বাক্য: 'A computer lab is a modern facility in the school. It contains several computers, printers and a projector for teaching.'

খ. (b) এর স্থানে কোন পূর্বপদ/প্রত্যয় ব্যবহার করবেন?

ক a
খ for
গ some
ঘ a

Explanation:
ক: 'variety of snacks' এর আগে অসংজ্ঞায়ক নিবন্ধ 'a' চলে: 'a variety of snacks' (অর্থ: বিভিন্ন ধরনের নাস্তা)।

খ: 'the students' কে সুবিধা দেয়ার ক্রিয়া বোঝাতে 'for the students' ব্যবহার করা প্রয়োজন — এখানে 'for' একটি পূর্বপদ (preposition): 'for the students'.

ঘ: 'pay a reasonable price' — 'reasonable price' এখানে একটি একক ধারণা হিসেবে ব্যবহৃত হচ্ছে, তাই 'a' নিবন্ধ ব্যবহার করা হয়: 'pay a reasonable price'.

পূর্ণ বাক্য: 'The school canteen provides a variety of snacks for the students. Students should buy some healthy food and pay a reasonable price for items.'

Question #167 (ID: 506832)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Our flat sits on (a) ______ top floor of (b) ______ old building beside (c) ______ central market. At night we worry about (d) ______ thieves, so we always bolt (e) ______ main door and check (f) ______ corridor for (g) ______ suspicious shadows before going to (h) ______ bed.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a) and (b).
খ. Fill blanks (c) and (d).
গ. Fill blanks (e) and (f).
ঘ. Fill blanks (g) and (h).


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the top floor; (b) an old building
খ (c) the central market; (d) thieves
গ (e) the main door; (f) the corridor
ঘ (g) a suspicious shadow; (h) bed

Explanation:
ক — (a) 'the top floor': we use 'the' because 'top floor' is a unique, definite position in that building; the speaker lives on that specific top floor. (b) 'an old building': 'old' begins with a vowel sound, so 'an' is required; it's nonspecific (one among many buildings). 

খ — (c) 'the central market': this is a particular market near the flat (definite), so 'the' is appropriate. (d) 'thieves': after 'worried about' we normally use the plural noun without an article when speaking generally about people of that type. Saying 'about thieves' (no article) means thieves in general. 

গ — (e) 'the main door': a specific door of their flat, so 'the'. (f) 'the corridor': we check the corridor of the building we live in (a specific corridor), so 'the' fits better than 'a'. 

ঘ — (g) 'a suspicious shadow': we use 'a' because it introduces one unspecified instance of a suspicious shadow. (h) 'bed': in everyday speech it's common to say 'go to bed' without an article. Using no article conveys the idiomatic meaning of sleeping.

Question #173 (ID: 506808)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Public Wi‑Fi hotspots are commonly found in coffee shops, airports, hotels and libraries. They allow devices to access the internet without using a cellular data plan. Hotspots rely on a local wired connection and a wireless access point, and many offer basic protection for users' traffic. Fill the blanks below about how hotspots work and what they require.

Options:
ক. Hotspots provide internet access to __________ users within a limited physical range.
খ. Hotspots normally connect to the internet over a __________ backbone provided by an Internet service provider.
গ. The wireless device that broadcasts the network to users is called an __________ (standards: IEEE 802.11).
ঘ. To encrypt user traffic on an open network, hotspots may implement security protocols such as __________ or __________.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক nearby mobile or portable device users

খ fixed wired broadband backhaul (e.g., DSL, cable or fiber)

গ Wi‑Fi access point (IEEE 802.11 AP)

ঘ WPA2 or WPA3 (Wi‑Fi Protected Access versions)

Explanation:
ক: Hotspots serve devices that are physically close to the access point — typically mobile phones, tablets, and laptops — so describing them as 'nearby mobile or portable device users' captures that limited range.

খ: A hotspot itself is an access layer; it forwards traffic to the wider internet over a fixed wired connection (DSL, cable, or fiber) supplied by a local ISP. Calling this the 'fixed wired broadband backhaul' is accurate.

গ: The device that creates the wireless network is an access point using the Wi‑Fi family of standards (IEEE 802.11). It may be built into a router or be a standalone AP.

ঘ: WPA2 and WPA3 are the current Wi‑Fi security protocols used to encrypt traffic and authenticate users on wireless networks. They are widely implemented to protect against eavesdropping on public hotspots.

Question #174 (ID: 506809)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Satellite phones and satellite data terminals provide communication where terrestrial networks are absent. They connect via orbiting satellites and are used in maritime, emergency, and remote-land operations. Complete the statements about satellite connectivity and performance.

Options:
ক. Satellite handsets communicate with __________ located above the Earth rather than with local cell towers.
খ. These systems are particularly valuable for __________ operations such as disaster response, scientific expeditions, and shipping.
গ. They are essential where there is no __________ infrastructure on the ground.
ঘ. One trade-off for wide-area coverage is often greater __________ compared with terrestrial cellular voice/data.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক communication satellites in orbit (GEO, MEO or LEO)

খ emergency, maritime and remote-area operations

গ terrestrial/cellular ground infrastructure

ঘ propagation delay (higher latency)

Explanation:
ক: Satellite phones link to satellites (which may be geostationary, medium-Earth, or low-Earth orbit) rather than to nearby terrestrial cell towers.

খ: Satellite systems are most useful where reliable terrestrial service is unavailable — for disaster relief, ships at sea, polar or desert expeditions, and other remote-area use cases.

গ: In those remote regions, the usual ground-based network elements (cell towers, wired backhaul) are absent or impractical, so satellites provide the missing connectivity.

ঘ: Signals must travel much farther to and from satellites, especially GEO satellites ~36,000 km up, introducing noticeable propagation delay (latency) compared with local cellular links; even LEO systems have some added delay relative to a purely terrestrial connection.

Question #175 (ID: 506810)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Smartphones integrate multiple technologies to offer voice, messaging, web browsing and a large ecosystem of third‑party applications. They rely on underlying platform services, distribution channels, location technologies, and user authentication. Fill in the blanks describing these components.

Options:
ক. The software layer that manages hardware, apps and resources on a phone is called the __________.
খ. The centralized online marketplace where users download apps is typically referred to as the __________.
গ. Built‑in receivers such as __________ provide location services for maps and navigation.
ঘ. Modern phones often use __________ (e.g., fingerprint or facial recognition) for secure local authentication.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক mobile operating system (e.g., Android or iOS)

খ app store / application marketplace (e.g., Google Play, Apple App Store)

গ GPS/GNSS receivers (Global Positioning System or other GNSS)

ঘ biometric authentication methods such as fingerprint or face recognition

Explanation:
ক: The mobile operating system (OS) — like Android or iOS — is responsible for managing CPU, memory, peripherals, app lifecycle, and security on smartphones.

খ: App distribution is handled via an app store or marketplace maintained by the platform vendor (for example Google Play on Android or the App Store on iOS), which provides installation, updates, and review controls.

গ: Location-aware features rely on GNSS receivers (commonly GPS) built into the device; these chips receive signals from navigation satellites to calculate position.

ঘ: To secure access, devices increasingly rely on biometrics (fingerprint sensors or front-facing facial-recognition systems) because they provide convenient and strong user authentication tied to the physical user.

Question #179 (ID: 506763)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A young painter inherited a tiny studio from her grandmother but lost interest in painting. She read novels instead of working at easels and left most of her supplies untouched. One afternoon she met (a) ___ elderly curator who advised her to take (b) ___ outdoor sketching class and practise every day. Following (c) ___ curator's advice, she cleaned (d) ___ brushes, primed (e) ___ canvases and began to paint. After several months she placed (f) ___ portfolio in (g) ___ local gallery and slowly regained her confidence.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(e).
গ. Fill blanks (f)–(g).
ঘ. Explain why the chosen articles/determiners are correct in one sentence each.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) an; (b) an; (c) the

খ (d) the; (e) the

গ (f) a; (g) the

ঘ Explanations:
- (a) "elderly" begins with a vowel sound (e-), so use "an elderly curator." 
- (b) "outdoor sketching class" is introduced nonspecifically here, and "outdoor" begins with a vowel sound (o-), so "an" fits the sound pattern; additionally, the curator is recommending one class among many: "an outdoor sketching class." 
- (c) The curator has been mentioned specifically now (the particular curator who advised her), so use "the curator." 
- (d) "the brushes" refers to the painter's own brushes already mentioned as untouched supplies, so the definite article "the." 
- (e) "the canvases" similarly refers to the painter's specific canvases in her studio. 
- (f) "a portfolio" is introduced for the first time and is nonspecific, so use "a." 
- (g) "the local gallery" points to a definite, contextually identified gallery (the one local to her), so use "the."

Explanation:
This passage tests correct use of articles (a/an/the) and definiteness. Use "a/an" for introducing something nonspecific or one among many; choose "an" before vowel sounds. Use "the" when referring back to a specific, previously mentioned, or contextually identifiable noun (e.g., the curator who advised her; the brushes and canvases in her studio; the local gallery known in context).

Question #180 (ID: 506764)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A retired gardener spent his mornings tending to (a) ___ vacant plot near (b) ___ river. He planted saplings there without expecting (c) ___ immediate return; he simply wanted to bring life to the place. One summer, (d) ___ stray dog started sleeping under (e) ___ young trees and the neighbors noticed. They offered (f) ___ cold drinks and asked if they could help water (g) ___ plants once a week.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(e).
গ. Fill blanks (f)–(g).
ঘ. Give a short justification (one sentence) for each filled article/determiner.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) the; (b) the; (c) an

খ (d) a; (e) the

গ (f) some; (g) the

ঘ Explanations:
- (a) "the vacant plot" — the plot is specific in the story (near the river), so "the." 
- (b) "the river" — a particular river referenced by location (near the plot), so definite article "the." 
- (c) "an immediate return" — introducing the idea of any single immediate return (nonspecific), so "an." 
- (d) "a stray dog" — a dog appears for the first time and is nonspecific, so "a." 
- (e) "the young trees" — these are the specific saplings the gardener planted, so "the." 
- (f) "some cold drinks" — plural, indefinite offer; "some" expresses an unspecified quantity of refreshments. 
- (g) "the plants" — refers back to the particular plants in the vacant plot, so the definite article "the."

Explanation:
Use "the" when both speaker and listener can identify the noun (specific plot, river, or the plants already planted). Use "a/an" for first mention of a singular, nonspecific item (a stray dog, an immediate return). Use "some" for an indefinite plural or uncountable quantity offered (some cold drinks).

Question #181 (ID: 506765)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
A traveler stopped at (a) ___ remote village and was invited to have (b) ___ cup of tea. He thanked (c) ___ host and walked up (d) ___ nearby hill. From the top he saw (e) ___ panorama of fields and rivers so striking that he decided to sketch it in (f) ___ small notebook. Before leaving he promised to send (g) ___ postcard to (h) ___ friend who loved landscapes.

Options:
ক. Fill blanks (a)–(c).
খ. Fill blanks (d)–(f).
গ. Fill blanks (g)–(h).
ঘ. Briefly explain why each article/determiner was used (one sentence per blank group).


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক (a) a; (b) a; (c) the

খ (d) the; (e) a; (f) a

গ (g) a; (h) his

ঘ Explanations:
- (a) "a remote village" — first mention, nonspecific, so "a." 
- (b) "a cup of tea" — an individual cup introduced for the first time, nonspecific: "a." 
- (c) "the host" — now refers to the specific person who invited him (definite), so "the." 
- (d) "the nearby hill" — a particular hill identified by proximity, so "the." 
- (e) "a panorama" — one among many possible views, introduced nonspecifically, so "a." 
- (f) "a small notebook" — a single notebook introduced nonspecifically for sketching, so "a." 
- (g) "a postcard" — one postcard, nonspecific; "a" is used for first mention. 
- (h) "his friend" — the friend is specific and related to the traveler; the possessive "his" makes it definite.

Explanation:
Articles 'a/an' introduce nonspecific, first-mentioned items; 'the' marks contextually specific or previously identified items. Possessives (his) inherently specify the noun (friend) and replace the need for an article.

--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Modern mobile devices do much more than make voice calls. A typical smartphone offers telephony, messaging, and internet services to (a) —— users moving across coverage areas. When a device leaves one coverage area and enters another, the connection is handed over between (b) —— that serve each cell. These radio access nodes forward calls and packets to an operator's (c) —— which provides switching, billing and interconnection to the public telephone network and the internet. Advances in radio and core design increased the available (d) ——, enabling services such as HD voice, video streaming and real‑time cloud apps.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a) — what kind of users?
খ. Fill blank (b) — name the radio nodes that cover cells.
গ. Fill blank (c) — what part of the operator's infrastructure handles switching and interconnection?
ঘ. Fill blank (d) — what was increased to enable streaming and real‑time apps?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক mobile users
খ base stations (cell towers / base transceiver stations)
গ core network (mobile core / IMS / EPC depending on generation)
ঘ data rates (bandwidth / throughput)

Explanation:
ক — "mobile users" is the standard term for people using wireless devices while moving between coverage areas. খ — The radio nodes that provide coverage for each cell are commonly called base stations; terms include cell towers or base transceiver stations (BTS). These perform the air interface functions and manage radio resources. গ — The operator's core network (for example, the EPC in LTE or the IMS for multimedia services) performs switching, subscriber management, billing, and interconnection with the PSTN and the internet. ঘ — To support services like HD voice and video streaming the networks increased available data rates (more bandwidth and higher throughput), achieved through better radio technologies, spectrum, and core capacity.

Question #195 (ID: 506671)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Consider portable wireless handsets used for personal and business communication. Unlike a desk phone that requires a physical phone jack, a handset registers using a subscriber identity stored on a (a) —— which authenticates the user to the operator. Calls and data are carried over the radio link to the nearest (b) —— and then through signaling and routing in the operator's backbone. Newer mobile services also support IP‑based voice (VoIP) over mobile — commonly called (c) —— — and features like mobile payments and push e‑mail rely on (d) —— for secure transactions.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a) — what stores subscriber identity?
খ. Fill blank (b) — name the immediate radio access node.
গ. Fill blank (c) — what is IP‑based voice over mobile networks called?
ঘ. Fill blank (d) — what is required to make mobile payments and push e‑mail secure?


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক SIM (Subscriber Identity Module)
খ base station (cell site)
গ VoLTE (Voice over LTE) or more generally VoIP over mobile
ঘ end‑to‑end security (encryption / secure authentication such as TLS / SIM‑based authentication)

Explanation:
ক — The SIM card holds the subscriber identity (IMSI and authentication keys) and enables the handset to register with the mobile network. Modern eSIMs perform the same function in embedded form. খ — The base station (also called cell site or eNodeB in LTE terminology) is the radio access point that connects the handset to the operator network. গ — IP‑based voice over mobile networks is commonly referred to as VoLTE in LTE networks; more broadly it is VoIP on mobile. VoLTE uses the IMS architecture for call control. ঘ — Secure mobile services require encryption and strong authentication. Techniques include SIM‑based authentication, TLS/HTTPS for apps, and payment‑specific protections (tokenization, secure elements) to ensure confidentiality and integrity.

Question #196 (ID: 506672)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
In areas without terrestrial cell coverage, specialized devices provide voice and data via satellites. Satellite phones connect to a (a) —— in orbit instead of a nearby cell tower. Compared with terrestrial cellular links, satellite links typically exhibit higher (b) —— which can affect interactive services. Their usable (c) —— is often lower than urban mobile networks, limiting high‑speed streaming, but they offer critical connectivity for (d) —— such as remote field teams and disaster response.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a) — what do satellite phones connect to?
খ. Fill blank (b) — what characteristic is higher on satellite links?
গ. Fill blank (c) — what resource is usually lower than in urban mobile networks?
ঘ. Fill blank (d) — name the groups that particularly benefit from satellite connectivity.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক satellite (satellite constellation / geostationary or LEO satellite)
খ latency (propagation delay)
গ bandwidth (data throughput)
ঘ emergency responders, remote workers, maritime and aeronautical users

Explanation:
ক — Satellite phones link to satellites (either a single geostationary satellite or a low‑earth‑orbit constellation) rather than terrestrial base stations. খ — Because of the long distances (especially to geostationary orbit), satellite communications generally have higher latency (longer propagation delay), which impacts real‑time interactivity like gaming or some VoIP scenarios. ল — Satellite systems often provide lower usable bandwidth compared with dense urban cellular networks, limiting sustained high‑speed streaming or large downloads. ঘ — Satellite connectivity is vital for emergency responders, remote field teams, ships, and aircraft where terrestrial networks are unavailable; it provides continuity of communication in disasters and remote operations.

Question #197 (ID: 506679)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
My father is (a) — honest and (b) — devoted family man. He works (c) — a factory and comes home (d) — the evening to spend time with us.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a)
খ. Fill blank (b)
গ. Fill blank (c)
ঘ. Fill blank (d)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an
খ a
গ in a factory
ঘ in the evening

Explanation:
ক (an): 'honest' begins with a vowel sound /ˈɒnəst/, so we use the indefinite article 'an'.
খ (a): 'devoted' begins with a consonant sound, so the correct indefinite article is 'a' — 'a devoted family man'.
গ (in a factory): For workplaces like 'factory' we commonly use the preposition 'in' to indicate being inside that place: 'works in a factory'. 'At a factory' is also possible but 'in a factory' emphasizes working inside the building.
ঘ (in the evening): The habitual time expression uses 'in the evening' to indicate a part of the day when he comes home.

Question #198 (ID: 506680)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
Our school has (a) — responsible headmistress. She treats students (b) — fairness and insists on (c) — highest standards. Students attend assemblies (d) — every morning.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a)
খ. Fill blank (b)
গ. Fill blank (c)
ঘ. Fill blank (d)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a
খ with
গ the
ঘ every

Explanation:
ক (a): 'responsible' begins with a consonant sound; use the indefinite article 'a' before a singular count noun: 'a responsible headmistress'.
খ (with): The phrase 'treats students with fairness' uses the preposition 'with' to link the verb 'treats' and the noun 'fairness'. Alternatively, one could say 'treats students fairly' (an adverb), but the blank as given suits 'with'.
গ (the): 'highest standards' refers to specific, highest level expectations, so the definite article 'the' is used: 'insists on the highest standards'.
ঘ (every): Time frequency 'every morning' does not take an article; the correct word is 'every' to indicate each morning.

Question #199 (ID: 506681)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
There is (a) — old banyan tree in the courtyard. Birds build nests (b) — its branches. Children play (c) — shade and read books (d) — afternoons.

Options:
ক. Fill blank (a)
খ. Fill blank (b)
গ. Fill blank (c)
ঘ. Fill blank (d)


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক an
খ on
গ in the shade
ঘ in the afternoons

Explanation:
ক (an): 'old' starts with a vowel sound, so use 'an' — 'an old banyan tree'.
খ (on): Birds build nests 'on its branches' because nests are placed on the surface of branches; the preposition 'on' denotes that location.
গ (in the shade): 'Play in the shade' is the idiomatic phrase using the preposition 'in' plus the definite article 'the' for a specific area of shade provided by the tree.
ঘ (in the afternoons): To indicate habitual activity during that part of the day, use 'in the afternoons' (or 'in the afternoon' for a general statement); 'in the afternoons' emphasizes repeated events across afternoons.

Question #200 (ID: 506631)
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Type: CQ | Book: English 2nd Paper | Years:  | Boards:  | Tags: 
--------------------------------------------------------------------------------
Question:
After you conduct a quick baseline check of student performance, you must decide which topics and activities to include in your next unit. Those decisions should reflect learners' current status as well as the goals you set. Many teachers treat content selection and assessment planning as separate tasks, yet they are closely linked and should inform one another throughout the instructional cycle.

Options:
ক. Choose the best word to complete: After you conduct (a) __________ baseline check of student performance...
খ. Choose the best word to complete: ...decide which topics and activities to include in (b) __________ next unit.
গ. Choose the best word to complete: Many teachers treat content selection and assessment planning as (c) __________ tasks...
ঘ. Choose the best word to complete: ...yet they are closely linked and should (d) __________ one another throughout the instructional cycle.


Correct Answer: 

Solution:
ক a
খ the
গ separate
ঘ inform

Explanation:
ক (a → a): The phrase 'a baseline check' introduces one instance of a screening activity; the indefinite article 'a' is appropriate because this is not specifying a previously mentioned unique baseline check. খ (b → the): 'the next unit' refers to a definite, specific unit that follows in the course sequence; 'the' identifies that particular upcoming unit. গ (c → separate): Grammatically and semantically, 'separate tasks' correctly conveys that teachers often treat these activities as distinct from each other. ঘ (d → inform): 'Inform one another' expresses the reciprocal relationship between content selection and assessment planning—each should provide input to the other. Pedagogically, this highlights alignment: assessments should reflect content and objectives, and content should be chosen with assessment and learning goals in mind.
